name: Glintstone Dragon Smarag | Elden Ring Wiki
Glintstone Dragon Smaragis aGreater Foe BossinElden Ring. Glintstone Dragon Smarag is a powerful magicdragonwith magic-stone formations for scales. ThisElden Ring Glintstone Dragon Smarag Guidefeatures boss locations, tips, strategies and videos on how to defeat Smarag easily, as well as boss stats and lore for Smarag. Bosses are unique and challengingEnemiesthat can be encountered all over the Lands Between. Great Enemy bosses can drop uniqueSpirit Ashes,Weapons,Spells, and other variousItems. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance inElden Ring.
Glintstone Dragonis the normal enemy form of this boss.
Smarag was a devourer of sorcerers, and over time, his body became corrupted by their glintstones.
From theCrystalline WoodsSite of Grace, head due south around the front of the craggy island in the lake. From theTemple QuarterSite of Grace, head due north and you'll eventually run into Smarag. [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
Defeating Smarag unlocksSmarag's Glintstone Breathat theCathedral of Dragon Communionin Caelid
SeeFlying Dragon Agheelfor a full boss guide
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
The Best Tips for Glintstone Dragon Smarag:
UseBanished Knight Olegfor his high defense and health to distract the dragon
Smarag has very high Magic resistance, so Intelligence builds should use spells likeRock Slingthat deal physical damage.
Meteorite of AstelwithCerulean Hidden Tearcan easily trivialize the fight by raining meteorites that deal physical damage.
Wear armor with high Magic and Physical resistance, like theBanished Knight Set
As this is an outdoors encounter, you can mountTorrentto quickly evade Smarag's breath attacks.  Melee users are encouraged to use Torrent to quickly get back into melee range when Smarag flies away.
Slaying this dragon allows one to buySmarag's Glintstone Breathat theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelid
Superior incantation of Dragon Communion.Channels the power of Smarag, the Glintstone Dragon.
Transforms caster into a dragon to spew magic breath from above.Charging extends duration. This incantation can be used while jumping.
One of the incantations of Dragon Communion.
Dragonis an enemy and category of boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Paltry, mortal descendants of theAncient Dragons[1]who once ruled theLands Between. They did not inherit their ancestors' command over lightning, and are instead vulnerable to it.[2]They typically possess  large wings in the place of front limbs. They have lost the stone scales possessed by their ancient kin, which can now be used to cause them mortal harm.[3]
Dragons are the offspring of Greyoll, a vast Dragon who dwarfed all who stood before her.[4]Greyoll, along with some of her children, escaped theScarlet Rotby settling on the plateau in the north ofCaelid, which became known asGreyoll's Dragonbarrow.[5]However, Greyoll appears to have succumbed to the rot, and can no longer take flight.
Dragons became the prey of hunters. Their hearts in particular were sought after by those who practiced Dragon Communion, who gained overwhelming power by consuming them.[6]Those who partook in Dragon Communion would eventually becomeMagma Wyrms, cursed to crawl the earth upon their bellies.[7]
Dragons who settled in northern Caelid with their mother, Greyoll. They surround the colossal Elder Dragon, who is now too decrepit to fight.
There are six red-eyed Flying Dragons surrounding Greyoll. Greyoll will lose 20% of her health with each Dragon killed, meaning that killing five will cause Greyoll to die.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Dragons imbued with glintstone, who roost atop the Moonlight Altar in westernLiurnia of the Lakes. They can emit glintstone breath, which inflictsmagicdamage.
These Dragons do not respawn when killed.
A Flying Dragon encountered in Agheel Lake in southern Limgrave, north-west of theDragon-Burnt Ruins. It appears by flying down from above, torching a congregation ofWandering Nobleswith dragonfire.
Nobles in the ruins around the lake, chanting Agheel's name, praying that it will burn them to ash.[8]
Bloody Finger Hunter Yurais available as a summon for this fight, after speaking to him under the ruin south of the lake.
Defeating Flying Dragon Agheel will unlockAgheel's Flame, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor twoDragon Hearts.
A devourer of sorcerers, whose body gradually became corrupted by the glintstones of those he ate.[9]Smarag is encountered near an island west of theAcademy of Raya Lucariaand north of theTemple Quarter, guarding a corpse that holds theAcademy Glintstone Key. Note that it isnotnecessary to kill this dragon to get the Academy Glintstone Key; it can be retrieved by either sneaking behind it or rushing beyond it before it's fully awakened to get at the corpse.
Smarag is able to fireGlintstone Cometshardsfrom his mouth, and can also unleash magic breath, akin to the fire breath of other Dragons.
Defeating Glintstone Dragon Smarag will unlockSmarag's Glintstone Breath, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor twoDragon Hearts.
A devourer of sorcerers, whose body became corrupted by glintstone. Adula was once bested byRanni the Witch, and subsequently swore a knightly oath to her Dark Moon.[10]
Adula is first encountered outsideRanni's Risein the Three Sisters, north ofCaria Manor. After a brief fight it disappears, only to reappear at the Moonlight Altar, outside theCathedral of Manus Celes.
Adula can use magic breath, much like Smarag, however it can also utiliseAdula's Moonblade, conjuring a magic blade in its maw mid-flight and unleashing a wave that inflictsFrostbite.
A Flying Dragon encountered on the Farum Greatbridge, on the northern peninsula of Greyoll's Dragonbarrow. Greyoll is identical to Agheel in both appearance and ability, however the bridge gives the player much less room to manoeuvre.
A massive but stationary dragon encountered inGreyoll's Dragonbarrow, just south ofFort Faroth. She is immobile, either having grown too weak to move or as a result of having fused with the surrounding rocks, but can still let loose fearsome roars to weaken her enemies.
Greyoll is known as the mother of the lesser dragon.[11]
Defeating any the six lesser dragons surrounding her will cause large amounts of damage to her, and killing them all will kill her.
Defeating Elder Dragon Greyoll will unlockGreyoll's Roar, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor threeDragon Hearts.
While the intended method of defeating her is by killing the surrounding lesser dragons, killing Greyoll herself directly through another method, such asBlood Loss, will also kill these smaller dragons. This method will also effectively give another 20,000 runes, making this an excellent place to use aGold-Pickled Fowl Footfor more runes early on.
A Dragon plagued by Scarlet Rot, encountered north-west of theCathedral of Dragon Communion. Also known as the Dragon Communion Revenger, Ekzykes did not forget his hatred even as he succumbed to the rot.[12]

Glintstone Dragonis the normal enemy form of this boss.
Adula, a devourer of sorcerers, was bested by Ranni and subsequently swore a knightly oath to her Dark Moon.

The Best Tips for Glintstone Dragon Adula:
Adula has very high Magic resistance, so Intelligence builds should use spells likeRock Slingthat deal physical damage.
Meteorite of AstelwithCerulean Hidden Tearcan easily trivialize the fight by raining meteorites that deal physical damage.
Wear armor with high Magic and Physical resistance, like theBanished Knight Set.
Adula was a devourer of sorcerers, but was defeated byRanni, after which they swore an oath to serve her, which explains why it appears in places relating to Ranni’s questline.
The name Adula is a reference to the scientific name, Adularia, of the semi-precious gem moonstone and the mountain in the Swiss Alps, Adula, where moonstone was first found.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Dragonkin Soldier | Elden Ring Wiki
Dragonkin Soldieris aBossinElden Ring. These giant decayed imitations of dragons dwell underneath the earth. ThisElden Ring Dragonkin Soldier Guidefeatures boss locations, tips, strategies and videos on how to defeat the Dragonkin Soldier easily, as well as boss stats and lore for the Dragonkin Soldier. Bosses are unique and challengingEnemiesthat can be encountered all over the Lands Between. Great Enemy bosses can drop uniqueSpirit Ashes,Weapons,Spells, and other variousItems. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance inElden Ring. However, doing so yields useful items, as well asRunes.
See alsoDragonkin Soldier of NokstellaandLesser Dragonkin Soldier (Spirit).
Alas, the Dragonkin Soldiers never attained immortality, and perished as decrepit, pale imitations of their skyborn kin.
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
At the start of the fight, the boss is slow to get up, which can allow one to get multiple hard hits in. This can take away a third to half of its HP right off the bat
UseSpirit Jellyfish Ashesto distract the boss, since it has a lot of health. If you have obtainedLatenna's Spirit Ash, you can place her out of range which allows her to steadily damage the boss from afar.
Night Maiden's Mistis a good way to get in some extra damage, since the Dragonkin Soldier is large and will tend to stay in contact with the cloud for a long time.
Ankle Biter:Stay near its legs as much as possible, where few of its attacks will damage you. Take care to avoid running or dodging forward towards its the stomach, since melee weapons without a particularly long reach tend to get blocked by its large belt. Instead, move forward and to the left or right to reach the Soldier's elbows or knees. Even when it turns around, you'll usually have enough time to run around its side and continue attacking. The main attacks to watch out for are Two-Hand Slam and Deep Slam, which create large enough shockwaves to hit you even at its feet. When it starts raising its hands for one of these, back off and jump attack in as it finishes.
Circle and Strafe:Dragonkin Soldier's movements are quite slow, so if you keep a medium distance it should be fairly easy to tell when it's safe to start attacking and when you should prepare to dodge. Circle clockwise to give yourself a bit of a head start against its longest-ranged attacks, and be prepared to start running if it roars to begin its Charge attack. Consider usingBarricade Shieldto block any heavy attacks that you don't have time to dodge.
According to their item drops, they were born in the Eternal Cities, but unfortunately, they never attained immortality like thestone-scaled dragonsof the surface and soon perished as mere imitations.The ones you meet are most likely reanimated corpses, as they are covered in wraps and their bodies have little to no flesh within.
Head south from theWorshippers' WoodsSite of Grace to a collapsed pillar with anAncestral Followerarcher perched on it. Follower the pillar up to its base, where you'll see the Siofra River East waygate. [Map Link] This waygate will transport you to the plateau in the center of Siofra River. When you arrive, head northwest to the open plain of shallow water, where you'll find the Dragonkin Soldier collapsed in a heap. As you approach, it will rise up and the fight will begin. [Map Link]You can also reach this boss from theAncestral WoodsSite of Grace by carefully dropping down from above.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Dragonkin Soldier has long reach and can quickly catch up to you if you try to stay too far away. Get too close, and it will slam the ground and cause shockwaves. But if you keep a medium distance, you can force it into a pattern where it uses close to mid range attacks which can easily be avoided on horseback by charging the boss and staying to your right. Even its left-hand arm swing will go over your head. You can get in several hits while the boss recovers from its attacks, and then dash back to medium range, rinse, and repeat.
Closest Site of Grace:Lake of Rot Shoreside
Head south-southeast from theLake of Rot Shoresideuntil you see the Dragonkin Soldier slumped over in the rot. If this is your first time approaching it, make sure to press the switch a short way to the east to raise a few platforms out of the rot so you can stand near it without getting infected. [Map Link]
Draw to Safety:In the far southeast corner of the lake, there's a ruin that rises well above the rot. Lure the Dragonkin Soldier to this location and climb onto the ruins to assault the Dragonkin Soldier from above while remaining safe from almost all its attacks.
Incantation that channels the power of the Dragonkin Soldiers.
Creates a spear of ice lightning and stabs it into the ground fromabove. On impact, the spear will burst into trails of lightning advancing forwards.
Dragonkin Soldieris a reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Dragon-like beings born in the Eternal City, they never knew true sky or true lightning, and so they wielded ice lightning as their weapon.[1]They never achieved immortality, and perished as decrepit imitations of trueAncient Dragons.[2]
They have humanoid bodies, with lanky arms and legs, and their chests have large, gaping cavities. They wear minimal armour, and red-and-black capes with golden embroidery.
Spectral Dragonkin Soldiers appear in theConsecrated Snowfield. They will disappear if the player gets too far away, and spawn continuously.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Draconic Tree Sentinel | Elden Ring Wiki
Draconic Tree Sentinelis an overworldBossinElden Ring. Draconic Tree Sentinel is a massive knight clad in golden armor that rides a massive horse and wields draconic magic.
Tree Sentinelis another version of this boss.
After the great ancient dragon Gransax attacked, the sentinels had an epiphany. The only way to truly protect the Erdtree was to become dragons themselves.
Capital Outskirts[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Crumbling Farum Azula[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Immune tocritical attacks. Breaking itsstanceorparryingit will only stun it briefly
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Enables entrance toLeyndell, Royal Capital.
GoldmaskandBrother Corhynwill disappear from the destroyed bridge atRoad of Inquity Site PathSite of Grace and move to their next location.
The Best Tips for Draconic Tree Sentinel:
Draconic Tree Sentinel met at Capital Outskirts does not move until it spots the player, what can be used to approach him from behind and deal some damage, f.e. by inflcitingScarlet Rot.
Consider summoning Tragoth and/or Millicent. They can provide decent damage and can take aggro away from you.
Use the Rotten Breath Spell for an easy kill.
Erdtree GreatshieldorCarian Retaliationcan parry the horse's fireballs.
If it's charging its shield for its lightning strike, roll the moment you see it pull the shield down.
As a general overview,Scarlet Rotis the best way to take down this boss, but if that's not accessible then Poison is second best and also strong. There is an easy cheese method to take him down that is 100% reliable and poses no risk. The cheese method is at the bottom.
Godrick's Great Runecoupled with aRune Arccan help you survive some one hit skills, such as the fireball or Shield Lightning skills.
Its AI is notorious for shooting fireballs whenever you are at medium-to-long range from it, and it's fond of using this attack as a heal-punish. If you remain at even medium distance from it, it's not unusual for this enemy to use this attack in quick succession until you get close enough for any of its melee attacks. If you need to heal, goad it into launching a fireball, dodge to the side, then heal. You will have just enough time to roll out of the way if it responds to your heal with a second fireball.
As of patch 1.03,Great Horned Tragothis available to summon for this fight. There are no triggers and he's available from level 1. This summon does ease the difficulty but it's by no means a walk in the park. Survival is the foremost priority. At least 20 Vigor, theKnight Armor,Boltdrake, andDragoncrest Shieldtalismans should prevent all one-shots and allow for flask use. Alternatively, have at least 20 Endurance and block his physical damage with any 100% physical resistant shield, usingPickled Turtle Neckfor stamina.
The key tactic of this fight is staying on the Sentinel's left side (your right) with the shield holding hand. While on his left, he attacks with a slower shield bash that's easier to dodge, does less damage, and allows room to counter attack. When his horse rears back, either for a fireball or stomp, is the best opportunity to roll to his left side. If using Tragoth, simply pause long enough for Tragoth to strike, this shifts his focus and you can safely flank the left/rear side.
Draconic Tree Sentinelis a recurring field boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Misshapen Tree Sentinels using a malformed golden armor adorned with various dragon imagery.
After the great ancient dragon Gransax attacked, the sentinels had an epiphany. The only way to truly protect the Erdtree was to become dragons themselves.[1]
TheirHoned Bolt-like overhead lightning strike has some unusual characteristics. It's unblockable (in fact, blocking will cause the character to take more damage as knockback is prevented and all 3 individual bolts of the attack will land) and cannot hit characters standing under the Sentinel's shield.

-Fia, Deathbed Companionabout the process of adding a new champion.
Throughout her life as aDeathbed Companionand her embraces of many,Fiahas accumulated small fragments of vigor from a litany of champions, so that their collective warmth may bring fallen exalted nobles or other people of importance back from the dead. These phantoms are the manifestation of those fragments and can be summoned by Fia even if the original champion they're sourced from is dead.
Upon arriving to the Prince of Dead's throne atDeeproot Depths, a Fia's Champion will invade the player. When defeated, a spectre ofSorcerer Rogieris summoned. Once he is felled two more "Fia's Champions" spawn, together with Lionel the Lionhearted.
Similar to the Knight of the Great Jar NPC enemies inCaelid, the three nameless NPC enemies are based on the character builds of other players. If playing offline, the default champions will appear.
If playing online, this champion will be replaced by a randomly selected player's character.

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Godskin Apostle | Elden Ring Wiki
Godskin Apostleis aGreat Enemy BossinElden Ring. These powerful and agile humanoids clothe themselves in the skin of gods and wield unique twinblades and black flame incantations. These are optional bosses as players are not required to defeat them to advance in Elden Ring.
Godskin Apostle also appears in theGodskin Duofight and as a spirit summon in aSpirit-Caller Snailfight.
The apostles, once said to serve Destined Death, are wielders of the god-slaying black flame. But after their defeat by Maliketh, the Black Blade, the source of their power was sealed away.
Godskin Apostle can be found in various locations:
Dominula, Windmill Village[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Divine Tower of Caelid[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Parryable: Yes, but 2 parries are required perstance break
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Use sleep pots with a strong spirit summon such asLhutel the Headless+4 to bait the Apostle to provide an opening for the pot to land. If the pot is a direct hit and he stays in the cloud, 1 pot will put him to sleep. If he exits the cloud, a second pot will put him to sleep (doesn't work with online players summoned). Use a bleed weapon with the BloodFlame enchantment, and land a 3x charged combo attack when he is sleeping to do more damage/ bleed build up than performing a critical hit would do. Do this a few times and the fight is done.
Maintain a medium distance from him at all times
UseGlintstone Stars,Glintblade Phalanxor any multi-hit spells that deal Magic damage to break his poise
The Godskin Apostle is a powerful boss equipped with a twinblade that has a sickle-end for slashing and a blade-end for thrusting and stabbing. He utilizes Black Flame spells similar to the monks earlier in the tower. When fighting this boss, you want to maintain a medium distance to avoid many of his attacks and only close in during openings. His melee attacks have a bit of weight to them and he does short wind-ups before attacking, similar to but not to the same extent as Margit at Stormveil.
Some notable attack windows are when he performs his Stab & Slash; he has a moderate recovery time after the second attack in which you can safely get one or two hits in. Another one is his Jumping Overhead Slash which has a slightly longer recovery than other attacks and can guarantee 2 hits for you. These two attacks are relatively easy to dodge. The attacks you should watch out for are his Black Flame as it travels quite quickly, you should dodge as soon as you see the casting rune; and his Stab & Pull which hits twice for massive damage. Another move he may use is the Spinning Weapon in which he twirls his blade in front of him as he advances forward. Maintain your distance or dodge through and behind him.
When his HP is lowered to 60%, he will float upwards briefly and then slam down, creating a shockwave around him, signifying his second phase. Get away from him when you see him float. From  this point, he can unlatch the skin of his upper torso from the rest of his body and fling it around to greatly extend his reach as well as unlock new abilities. His notable attack windows during this phase is when he uses the Flight variant of Spinning Weapon, in which he flings his upper torso outwards while spinning his weapon. His lower body remains stationary and if you can dodge through his weapon, he will be vulnerable to attack from his elongated abdomen to his legs for the duration of the attack as his torso is locked in the animation.
He will also frequently use a Plunging Blade & Sweep move where he flings his torso upwards and then slams down with his weapon, followed by a very wide sweeping slash. Both hits are easy to read and can be outranged or dodged and he is vulnerable for a couple of seconds after the sweep. Lastly, he can perform a Black Flame Whirlwind attack where he twirls his weapon in place, creating a whirlwind extending outwards all around him. The attack culminates with him plunging his blade into the ground and causing the whirlwind to burst and extend outwards a short distance from its initial edge. Do not stand too close to the edge even when the whirlwind has stopped moving.
The strategy for ranged players is largely the same and in fact, they may have an edge as the Apostle's attacks hit below medium range, which is where ranged players want to stay at anyway. The Godskin Apostle seems susceptible to magic damage and his poise can be broken rather easily by using multi-hit spells such asGlintblade PhalanxorGlintstone Stars, allowing you to get a critical attack in.
The Godskin Apostles' theme is not in Latin. The lyrics are mostly nonsensical latinish syllables and vowel sounds arranged in a way that makes them sound like Latin. This was confirmed by youtuber Antonius Tertius (aka redditor MAGISTER-ORGANI), a Latin scholar, who contacted some music producers and singers of Elden Ring and published the official lyrics and backstage information on his channel.
Among the official singers who recorded the Godskin Apostles' theme, there were no children as some believe. The sopranos were all adult women. This was confirmed by youtuber Antonius Tertius who contacted members of the choir hired by Bandai.
Along with their Noble comrades, they served the Gloam-Eyed Queen and wielded Black Flame to slay the gods and wear their skin.
Godskin Apostleis a reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Lanky humanoids clad in robes sewn together from patches of smooth skin.[1]The Godskin Apostles were led by theGloam-Eyed Queen[2], who cradled them as newborns in a swaddling cloth made from skin much like their robes[3]. They servedDestined Death[1], and wielded god-slaying black flame. However, whenMaliketh, the Black Blade, sealed away the Rune of Death, the flame's true power was lost.[4]

name: Godskin Noble | Elden Ring Wiki
Godskin Nobleis aGreat Enemy BossinElden Ring. These humanoid enemies dress in an armor made from voluminous flaps of skin, wielding rapiers and black flame magic. They are optional bosses as they don't need to be defeated to advance in Elden Ring.
Godskin Noble also appears in theGodskin Duofight and as a spirit summon in aSpirit-Caller Snailfight.
Nobles are the most ancient apostles who are said to have assimilated inhuman physiology. Not unlike the crucible, the Erdtree in its primordial form.
Godskin Noblecan be found in various locations:
Divine Tower of Liurnia[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Usesleep potsto put the boss to sleep. Usually one is enough and will allow you to get multiple hits in before it wakes up. Repeat as needed.
Alternatively,sleep arrowsare very easy to craft at the point of game when players meet Noble for first time.
The Godskin Noble is fast and can deal damage or break poise rapidly through the Stab and Overhead Strike, and Stab and Backhand attacks. Generally melee users should circle around the Noble to deal damage while avoiding combo attacks, and quickly back away when the Black Flame Barrier spell is telegraphed. Parrying is difficult and not necessarily critical given the Noble does not have significant resistances to physical attack. Simply dodge rolling and avoiding physical attacks while striking occasionally is generally enough to outlast the Noble.
Bleed, poison and rot may be applied to the Noble without significant difficulty but take care when doing so with short or midrange melee weapons as the Noble does use its shove, barrier, stomp and belly roll moves to distance the player character if too much damage is done at once. The belly roll may be stopped by striking the Noble during the roll which will interrupt the attack and provide an opening for followup attacks.
Bridge to Divine Tower of Liurnia: Once reaching his threshold that causes his attack pattern to change, the Godskin Noble will roll at the player. When he begins rolling, you can catch him in one of the ports on the side of the bridge so he gets stuck. If you're able to make it back to the entrance, you can go to one side and when he attempts to roll up the stairs he will angle over the guard rail and fall to his death.
For Incantation users, best is to inflict one of Status Effects at the start and then attack Noble with eitherLightning SpearorSwarm of Flies.
One met at Divine Tower of Liurnia can be baited to roll himself of the bridge and die.
This is an optional boss, although either it orJuno Hoslow, Knight of Bloodmust be defeated to proceed in Volcano Manor
From theGuest HallSite of Grace, head east across the lava and up the rooftops until you reach a stone platform with a cage elevator. Take the elevator up, go up the stairs, and activate the switch to lower the drawbridge back to thePrison Town ChurchSite of Grace. Then head up the last set of stairs into the church to fight the Noble. [Map Link]

Godskin Duois a boss battle where you have to battle against aGodskin ApostleandGodskin Nobleat the same time. They can be found inCrumbling Farum Azula. This isnotan optional boss as they must be defeated to advance further in Crumbling Farum Azula.
The Godskin Duo share one health bar of around 24000 HP (NG), but also still have their own HP. If one is killed, it will either respawn automatically after ~15 seconds or the other Godskin will reanimate them. They will also still enter phase 2 if dropping close to 50% in individual HP.
The pillars within the arena are an effective way to separate them, although their phase 2 attacks will demolish the upper portion of them. In addition, both of them can be parried.
Sleep Potscan serve as a way to buy time as both bosses can be rendered temporarily paralyzed by sleep status.

The Best Tips for Ancient Dragon Lansseax:
UseLatenna. Summon her far away from the boss and draw its attention away from her. She will deal steady damage to the boss but is quite frail and will not survive long if the boss is focused on her.Another good alternative is theAncestral Follower.
Use theShard Spiralspell, as her large hitbox means that the attack can land multiple times.
Bring someLightningproof Dried LiverandBoiledCrabfor damage negation.
Turn off camera lock, as it can only lock onto the head and body of the dragon, which can be very disorienting.
When facing this boss, do not take the lightning attacks lightly since they have the ability to one-shot players. While in the air, you may see a resemblance of a weapon made with lightning. At this point you need to back up to prepare to jump over this weapon attack or dodge. Ideally stay on higher or lower ground so you can go over or under some its attacks. For greater speed, you may want to consider seeing this fight through while on Torrent so you can be quick in disengaging when needed. This way you can wait for openings and also quickly run in with Torrent for a quick hit and escape if needed. This will lessen the chances of getting stepped on than if you were to run in on foot. While on Torrent, it will also give you enough time to run away from any anticipated fire attacks or landing spaces.
For attacks, Torrent will also be beneficial for reaching her head for attacks with his higher jumps, especially on higher ground. The main melee strategy is to keep moving and a combination of looking for openings to run in for a few hits and then running back out to repeat the process.
With ranged attack, and a big field going against a dragon with large range, it is still recommended to use Torrent for this fight to quickly cover distances either for escaping an attack or running in for a better angle.  Lots of the dragon's attack cover a large AoE. You will need to continuously disengage and move around to stay out of her line of sight and give yourself a better position to deal attacks. For range, it is a combination or circling back, stopping to get an angle and dealing an attack while anticipating her next attack and being prepared to back away. This may make it more difficult to aim with smaller ranged spells and attacks so you may still need to use Torrent to approach and get better angle to hit.
If you keep moving, there is a chance she will constantly be trying to turn towards you and repositioning rather than dealing attacks, which will give you more opportunities to keep attacking while moving until she is eventually cleared.
Ancient Dragonis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
The Ancient Dragons ruled in the prehistoric era before theErdtree.[1]They wielded red lightning as a weapon[2], and had scales made of sharp, pointed gravel stones.[3]They were ruled over byDragonlord Placidusax, said to have beenElden Lordin the time before the Erdtree[4], from the royal city ofFarum Azula[5], and it is said that they would protect their lord as a wall of living rock.[6]
Ancient Dragons have light grey bodies resembling stone. They possess four legs, as well as four wings inlayed with gold, distinguishing them from theirlesser descendants. They have short, flat muzzles, orange-yellow eyes, and wispy grey hairs along their backs. They can breathe fire like many of their descendants, however they also possess the ability to wield red lightning, which often manifests in the form of spears and glaives.
During the reign ofQueen Marika the Eternal, the Ancient Dragon Gransax wrought havoc onLeyndell, Royal Capital, the only time in recorded history that Leyndell's walls have fallen.[7]This marked the dawn of the war against the Dragons, during which the Tree Sentinels clad themselves in armor resembling the bodies of the Dragons in order to protect the Erdtree.[8]During this conflictGodwyn the Goldenfought to the last against the Ancient DragonFortissax.[9]Godwyn defeated Fortissax, however he befriended his fallen foe, ending the conflict and giving rise to the capital's Ancient Dragon Cult.[10]Worship of the Ancient Dragons does not conflict with faith in the Erdtree, as the Dragons' lightning is imbued with gold, and as such the Cult was permitted within Leyndell.[11]
Ancient Dragons are greatly resistant toStancedamage. In addition to their base 120 Stance health, they only take 20% Stance damage (effectively giving them 600 Stance health against those hits) from hits against everything except for their heads, though their heads at least take doubled Stance damage compared to the rest of their body (effectively giving them 300 Stance health against those hits). Though their Stance health won't refill unless they haven't taken Stance damage for a fairly lengthy 9.231 seconds, this, in addition to how hard their heads can be to hit, make them sturdy foes.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Lansseax, the sister of Fortissax, is said to have taken the form of a human priestess in order to commune with the knights of the Ancient Dragon Cult.[12]Her most beloved knight wasVykethe dragonspear[13], a Tarnished knight of theRoundtable Hold, who was later scourged by the frenzied flame.[14]
Lansseax is first encountered near the Abandoned Coffin Site of Grace, near the entrance to Altus Plateau from theRuin-Strewn Precipice. After sustaining enough damage, she will fly away. She can later be encountered on a hill just south-west of the Rampartside Path Site of Grace in the east of Altus Plateau, where she can be defeated for good.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.

The Full-Grown Fallingstar Beast is very similar toAstel, Naturalborn of the Void. Both are extraterrestrial creatures of rock, feature many sharp tail barbs, large mandibles, and heads with a central cracked hole revealing an eye underneath, along with using gravity magic.These beasts may be younger forms of Astel as there are manyMalformed Starsfound underground, and there are two Astels fought as bosses. If one looks closely at its eye, it slightly resembles the skull of an Astel.

Fallingstar Beastis a reoccurringbossinELDEN RING(2022)and.
Fallingstar Beasts are creatures formed of shiny black rock. They have spiky tails, patches of white fur, and insect-like mandibles. They are found in craters, likely indicating that they plummeted onto theLands Betweenfrom a great distance.
The more mature Full-Grown Fallingstar Beast have greater magical abilities, able to control gravity in their vicinity and unleash great magical beams akin toComet Azur.
They can use Gravity-based abilities, much like other enemies associated with meteors and fallen stars such asAlabaster Lords,Onyx Lords, andWithered Astel. Much like those other enemies, they are also weak to gravity-based sorceries. Additionally, extraterrestrial weapons such as theWing of Asteland theAlabaster Lord's Swordandgravity imbued weaponssuch as theStarscourge GreatswordandRadahn's Speargreatarrows deal bonus damage to these foes.

Regal Ancestor Spiritis aLegend BossinElden Ring. This animated carcass of a deer-like creature is encountered in theHallowhorn Groundsfound inNokron, Eternal City. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance inElden Ring.
Ancestral spirits exist as a phenomenon beyond the purview of the Erdtree. Life sprouts from death, as it does from birth. Such is the way of the living.
Ancestor Spirit is found in an isolated arena accessible from Nokron, Eternal City. To access it, you must light all six obelisks by the stairs to theHallowhorn Groundsnortheast of theAncestral WoodsSite of Grace. When you've done so, the deer carcass at the back of the temple will glow and you can interact with it to teleport just outside the boss's arena. Walk through the fog gate to fight the boss.

Ancestral spirits exist as a phenomenon beyond the purview of theErdtree. Life sprouts from death, as it does from birth. Such is the way of the living.
TheRegal Ancestor Spiritis an optionalRemembrancebossinELDEN RING(2022). It is encountered at the northernHallowhorn Groundsalong theSiofra Riverafter lighting six bonfires.
Deer-likespiritsfound inSiofra River. They exist beyond the purview of theErdtree, and follow the principle that life sprouts from death as it does from birth.[1]This process is reflected by theirhorns, which sprout new growths even after the ancestor's death.[2]Shamansof theAncestral Followersdonheaddressesfashioned from horns with buds, mirroring the appearance of the ancestor spirits.[3]
Ancestor Spirits appear emaciated, with exposed ribs, matted fur, and cavities in their chests. They have large, antler-like horns which glow and sprout small buds.
An Ancestor Spirit found in the upper part of Siofra River at the northernHallowhorn Grounds, north-east ofNight's Sacred Groundand theAncestral WoodsSite of Grace. Much like the otherAncestor Spirit, this one can only be fought after lighting flames- in this case six- in the surrounding area and then touching the horned remains.
Although it initially fights in much the same way as the standard Ancestor Spirit, once its health has been reduce to half it will start to heal itself by siphoning HP from the player, as well as from the spirit animals in the arena. It will also sometimes collapse and fade away, and then emerge from one of the other animals in the arena. It can also use abilities reminiscent of other animals- hopping like aspringhare, charging like aboar, or curling into a ball and rolling like agoat.

Magma Wyrmis a reoccurringbossinELDEN RING(2022).
Magma Wyrms are quadrupedal draconic beings with torn, vestigial wings and broad heads. They were once human heroes who partook in Dragon Communion, for which they were cursed to crawl the earth[1]as flightless imitations of Dragons, losing their humanity in the process.[2]They wield greatswords that resemble the jawbones of dragons, and can spew magma from their mouths.
Only one non-boss Magma Wyrm can be encountered. It is found in the lower part ofVolcano Manor, accessible via an elevator near the Temple of Eiglay Site of Grace.

Its attacks can inflict damage on theCrabsandLand Octopusnearby, which will cause them to aggro against it.

Metyr, Mother of Fingerscan be encountered in theFinger Ruins of Miyr, you may find her by entering theCathedral of Manus Metyrand interacting with the throne. The Mother received signs from the Greater Will from the beyond of the microcosm. Despite being broken and abandoned, she kept waiting for another message to come.
Metyr, Mother of Fingersis an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. She is encountered after ringing the bell at theFinger Ruins of Miyr, beneath theCathedral of Manus Metyr.
Metyr, brilliant daughter of theGreater Will, was the first of all stars to fall upon theLands Between.[1]She possessed a microcosm which allowed her to receive messages from the Greater Will.[2]Metyr gave birth to theTwo Fingersthat guide theempyreansand theTarnished.[1]
Metyr was damaged and is possibly the source of theRinged Finger.[3]She would never again receive a signal from the Greater Will.[2]The wisdom received by the Two Fingers was severed, and Metyr began birthing the aberrantFingercreepers.[1]Although Metyr was broken, her Two Fingers continued guiding the empyreans without a word from the Greater Will.[4]It is said they presided over the birth ofMarika’sErdtreeas she created it from the primordial matter of theCrucible.[5][6][7]
Count Ymirwas aglintstone sorcererwho became afinger-weaverand uncovered the secrets of Metyr herself.[8]He found Metyr concealed within the Finger Ruins of Miyr, below the Cathedral of Manus Metyr, still waiting in vain for a signal from her lord.[2]Ymir uncovered that Metyr's true power, and the guidance of the Two Fingers, had been broken long ago.[4][6]After Ymir's young childYuridied, his grief drove him to find a way to bring him back.[9]He decided he would succeed Metyr as the next mother of Fingers.[6]
Ymir shares the wisdom of the cosmos and aHole-Laden Necklacewith theTarnished champion. He directs them to sound the ominous hanging bells at theFinger Ruins of DheoandRhea. Once both bells are rung, Ymir reveals the location of the Ruins of Miyr. Ringing the third and final bell will leave one's fate guided by the stars—and face-to-face with Metyr. If the Mother of Fingers is defeated, Ymir's hope is rekindled but the prospect of achieving his dream drives him mad.[10]He achieves a partial transformation and fails to birth Yuri anew, instead creating more Fingercreepers.[11]
Metyr is a monstrous being made from fingers. Her head resembles an elongated thumb, and her face a pronounced thumbprint. At its center is a small, wart-like eye from which she blasts pink energy beams.[12]Ridge-like wrinkles, forming fingerprint-like patterns, cover Metyr's head and neck. She moves about on four sets of four-fingered hands, 16 coordinated finger legs in total. Metyr has two long-reaching arms that terminate in four-fingered hands tipped with sharp nails painted red. She may use these to pry open her abdominal cavity when birthing new Fingercreepers. Her tail forks into two tail fingers which wrap each other like a spiral. Between them rests an orb containing a microcosm.[2][13]
Metyr's body festers with unhealed wounds. Upon her right chest is a deep laceration, and her belly has been split wide open, revealing gore and the stillborn remains of malformed fingers. Several more protrude from large lesions on her neck and tail fingers, and her microcosm appears clouded like an eye with cataracts. The iris of her bloodshot eye is quartered into an X.[13]
Metyris an optional boss fight that can be fought by the end ofCount Ymir's questline; after blowing the two finger bells at the other finger ruins, and returning to the cathedral and examining Ymir's throne, she is found in theFinger Ruins of Miyr, just beneath theCathedral of Manus Metyr.
Metyr crawls around and can fire a laser beam from her eye. Try fighting her head-on. She punishes flanking during this phase.
Metyr summons her damaged microcosm and uses it to channel gravity magic. Be wary that she can fly during this stage, which can be troubling for some melee players.

Commander Gaiusis aLegend BossinElden Ring.Commander Gaiusrides a boar into battle and uses several magic attacks and is found at the back of theShadow KeepLegacy Dungeon. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance inShadow of the Erdtree.

Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.

Opt for aGreat Hammerlike theHeavy Curved Great Club
BringFlask of Wondrous Physick(Greenburst Crystal TearandOpaline HardtearorWindy Crystal Tear) Item
UseCrucible Feather Talismanto make dodging his charge easier
Before you begin the fight, make sure to replenish yourFlaskby resting at the nearest Site of Grace. You can also prepare your loadout by equipping theFlask of Wondrous Physickand using it with theGreenburst Crystal TearandOpaline Hardtearto give you a temporary boost to all damage negation and stamina recovery speed. Once these items are ready, you can now head towards the fight. As soon as you walk into the arena, make sure to summonBlack Knife Tiche. This is an Ash Summon with immunity to allStatus Effectsand is the ideal summon for this fight.
Commander Gaius rides a giant wild boar that can rush forward in great speed. You will be battling both the rider and the Wild Boar here, and they can combine their attacks as you take them on. For melee users, the key to this fight is heavy attacks and jump attacks. This trades off defense for a chance to break the boss' stance and deal additional damage. While fighting this boss, try to stick to its sides and back. This gives you the best chances to avoid getting damaged especially during the first phase. The boss doesn't use a lot of its gravity attacks early on but will rely mostly on Standard damage type with its weapon swings.
To begin, Commander Gaius will always open the fight with theWild Boar Rushas you enter the arena, which is a move where he charges at you as you enter the arena. You can dodge by rolling into him at the very last second. While you are near this boss, it can useWild Swingtogether with aKickandHead Slamfrom the wild boar. If you're feeling confident, you can roll towards the swing of the weapon, and toward the Wild Boar for the Head Slam. The kick is a little difficult to dodge because it gives very little time to react. However, you can anticipate this attack if you spend too much time attacking from behind. Each time the boss finishes its string of attacks, prepare for a heavy or jump attack. This is your chance for retaliation and an opportunity to break its stance.
The boss' second phase will begin once its health drops to about 50%. You will notice this when the boss clutches its body as the purple color mixed with lightning courses throughout his armor. During this phase, the boss will start using all of its gravity attacks and its basic attacks will deal additional gravity damage. These attacks are easily discernible because his weapon will glow purple, and you can hear a crackling audio cue as it charges up.
There are about 5 Gravity attacks that we saw when we took down this boss, and one of the most dangerous ones is theGravity Plunge. This is an attack that begins with a jump toward the sky, the boss will spin in place to charge the attack and plunge at high speed. The impact has a pretty wide AoE, so you shouldn't underestimate it. Ideally, you want to roll backward and away from the impact, but in situations where you prefer a high-risk/high-reward scenario, you can try to roll forward as the boss plunges and pull off a jump attack while the boss recovers from the impact.
The other gravity attack worth mentioning is theGravity Thrust, this is a move that he does where he charges up his weapon with gravity magic and then makes an upward thrust with it, creating an AoE damage within the area around him. When he does this, roll forward to dodge and you can retaliate with a light attack.
Gaius and Radahn were good rivals in their youth, and this
sorcery is a product of their friendly competition.-Blades of Stone
Commander Gaiusis abossinShadow of the Erdtree.
Gaius was a commander in the army ofMessmer the Impaler, and an Albinauric who relied upon a boar mount to compensate for his missing legs.[1]. Gaius was a friend to Messmer, as well as both an elder brotherly figure[2]and rival[3]ofRadahn. He was also the most senior disciple of the sameAlabaster Lordwho taught Radahn his gravitational techniques.[4]
Commander Gaius will charge with his boar to try to run you over. This can be dodge by jumping over with torrent or dodging at a very exact moment. He also uses gravity magic to attack enemies that are too far away.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Ash summons: Mimic Tear (to duplicate yourHoly Damageeffect)
Recommended armaments:Barbed Staff-Spear,Black Knife,Black Steel Greathammer
BringDrawstring Holy GreaseorHoly Greaseto increase Holy Damage

Other items:Glovewort Crystal Tear,Windy Crystal Tear,Holy-Shrouding Cracked Tear,Faith-knot Crystal Tear,Leaden Hardtear
This boss is weak toHoly Damage, but is not classified asUndead.
The Putrescent Knight rides a steed, though they do not share separate healthbar. The fight is made more challenging because of the horse, who assists the Knight in executing combos from time to time. Luckily, this boss is weak toHoly Damageand if you're having difficulty taking it down, consider making changes to your current build. For melee users, you want to make sure that you will stick close to the Putrescent Knight. This way, you will be able to chip away at its health every time there's an opening.
To begin, this boss can open the fight with one of its special moves. It will charge toward you and jump into the air, while the horse vanishes into the ground. The Knight will plummet in your direction and chop down with the cleaver, followed closely by a spin attack, then the horse will charge toward you, and then the knight will do another spin attack. There's a chance that the last 2 of this combo will be repeated where the horse will charge again, and the knight will do another spin. You can dodge this attack combo, by rolling forward as the knight plummets down with the cleaver. Pay attention to the knight here while he prepares for the spin attack, and then roll towards him as he spins to the right, then roll toward the horse before it makes an impact, and then roll right towards the knight. If the last 2 steps will be repeated, the horse will come from the right side. The same thing applies so you can either roll forward or roll to the right towards the horse and then roll toward the knight again. At the end of this attack, this boss will create distance between the two of you which makes it impossible to attack for melee users, in that case, you want to be ready with any ranged attack or spells that you can use, or wait for the next opening.
The next combo from this boss is theCleaver Chop attack. This is when he chops down with his weapon using both hands while he's on horseback. Be very careful as he can combine this move with quick sweeps on either side. There's a wind-up for this attack pattern, so make sure you keep an eye on his arm movements. When it comes to the chop down, you want to roll forward as soon as he strikes, then, for the quick sweeps, you will roll towards the origin of the weapon. You can either do it to the side (left or right) or forward, towards the boss.
All tainted flesh eventually becomes putrescence, and this clump of it imbibed St. Trina's nectar, which granted it eternal rest. And so it was that putrescence became her knight.

Thedefensenumbers are compared to the incoming attack power to determine how much to scale down the damage. The higher the ratio, the more damage comes through.
Thenegationnumbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through a nd 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
The Best Tips for Knight of the Solitary Gaol:
You should get Scadutree Blessing level 1 or 2 for an easier kill: SeeScadutree Fragmentfor the locations and where to find them
This boss can switch between aGreatswordand aCrossbowgiving him an edge in melee and ranged situations. The fight against the Blackgaol Knight usually begins with aCrossbowattack. He fires up to 10 Arrows rapidly following the player's movement and he requires a brief moment to either reload or switch to the Greatsword. There are some situations where his Arrow will have a fire element to it, which can end up damaging you even if you put your shield up. While he's firing the attack, you can run to one side diagonally, or horizontally and engage him in melee combat.
The crossbow gives him an advantage against melee users so it's ideal to stay within attacking distance by going up to him. You'll likely end up getting your HP drained without a fight if you stay far back while you have a melee weapon. You can also equip a shield to block his ranged attacks. At first, his attacks are slow and simple. He swings his greatsword with a powerful slash and you can stay out of his path by rolling to your right side. He holds up the sword with his right arm, and this direction gives you the biggest space to cut off his reach.
If you have a shield equipped, you can use it to block his incoming attacks or attempt a parry. Both of these methods will give an opening to attack him for maybe 1 or 2 attacks, depending on how fast your attack speed is. Opt for heavy attacks orAsh of War: Giant Hunt, or any Ash of War you prefer. This will cut him off in between combos. This can eventually applyStaggerif you repeatedly hit him with heavy attacks. This boss also has an attack that is similar to theVacuum Slicethat he can combine with another half-spin thrust. You can dodge this move by rolling to your right as he approaches you, then roll forward (towards him) to get behind him. From here, you have an opening to attack him with a heavy attack.
You will also notice that this boss tends to dojump attacks. If you can hit him while he's mid-air, you can knock him down and get free hits out of this opportunity. As the fight goes on, this boss will also restore its health using a Flask. You can interrupt him by using a spell likeAdula's Moonbladeto cancel the animation.
If you find yourself needing to restore HP, make sure to do it at a safe distance and that you have enough time. He may switch to the Crossbow or do aWide Slashattack that lets him close the gap to perform a melee attack. Another strategy here is to alternate using your shield and go on offense by attacking him as you move to your right. This will give you a moment to attack him from behind for increased damage and also makes you move away from his right weapon swings.
Keep distance from his sword swings and use spells that can get around his input reading by using well-timed casts or theNight Cometspell. Avoiding his crossbow attack can lead to a large opening.
The name of this boss was changed in an update from Blackgaol Knight to Knight of the Solitary Gaol.
May be a nod to 'the Black Swordsman' Guts from manga and anime series Berserk.
These knights, through a secret rite, relinquished their hearts for heightened battle prowess.
Knight of the Solitary Gaolis an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. They are encountered in theWestern Nameless Mausoleum.
The namelessspiritof a member of the Knights of the Solitary Gaol that lingers within a mausoleum in theRealm of Shadow.[1]These knights offered their hearts through esoteric rite, gaining heightened battle prowess. Their steel greatswords bear two carved emblems: one symbolizing the light of birth and the other, solitude.[2]
Wears a heavy set of overlapping steel armor:Armor of Solitude,Gauntlets of Solitude,Greaves of Solitude, and theHelm of Solitude. Wields aGreatsword of Solitudeand aRepeating Crossbow.

Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.

Recommended Summons:Mimic Tear,Black Knife Tiche Ashes
Recommended Skills:Lion's Claw,Savage Lion's Claw
Just like a Hippopotamus, this boss relies on the might of its bite and fights with its head. At the start, the boss will rush towards you withFanged Rush,a move that it uses to close the gap by charging forward with its mouth wide open. As the boss gets near you, it will try to devour you and slam its head on the ground multiple times. You can dodge this attack by sprinting to either side of the boss at an angle, then rolling away from its head at the last second. Dodge earlier than you would usually for attacks because the AoE is larger than it looks. If you get caught, you will be unable to move and you will be stuck inside its mouth. If you happen to have remaining HP after this move, the boss will throw you up.
Aside from the aggressive bites, this boss will also slam its head which can throw you off balance and because of the size of this boss, it is better to dodge toward its body and away from the head. This creates more distance from the head compared to rolling backward. The Golden Hippopotamus is weak to heavy attacks, and you need to keep an eye out for openings. The boss takes a few seconds of rest after it finishes a move. If you happen to break its poise, be patient and walk towards the head, and press R1 to deal additional damage.
This boss can also do the Belly Slam attack where you see it stand on its legs. This move has a long wind-up time and a slight delay before it slams its belly. For this move, the best way to dodge is to roll on either side, and you will be able to retaliate with an attack directly on its head. When the boss' health drops to 50%, it will create golden quills on its head and body. One of the changes that this will make is that, whenever the boss does theBelly Slam, its quills will rain from above. This will affect a small area around the boss and will deal damage if you stay there. Make sure to roll backward to keep out of the slam's AoE, then run horizontally to the Golden Hippopotamus to avoid the quills. The quills will also go away after a few seconds so be patient and wait for the quills to vanish and you can continue attacking the boss.
Lastly, one of the moves is theGolden Quill Air Strikewhich will rain down golden quills, or combine them with a spinning 360 attack. This move can be dodged by rolling twice backward in quick succession. The boss might follow up this move with another combo so make sure to pay attention to its next movements before you commit to doing any attacks after.
Sorcery users will find great success usingShard Spiral, as the size of the boss will have him get him multiple times by each spiral, taking massive damage. If you find the opening,Rellana's Twin Moonscan do massive damage and reduce the boss' magic resistance, but it's generally too risky to use this attack.
The same applies to incantation users, who can castPest Threadsto similar effect. If you find the opening,Burn, O Flame!is also a great option.
TheGolden Hippopotamusis an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. It is encountered at theShadow Keep.
Hippopotamiare giant quadrupeds that live near bodies of water. Several can be found in theRealm of Shadow. One particular specimen in theShadow Keep, called the Golden Hippopotamus, can grow thorn-like fur on its back; a vestige of the vitality of theCruciblewhich flourished before the land was enshrouded in shadow.[1]
A hungry, hungry hippo. It is much larger than the standard variants.
It has many area-of-effect abilities, but it is lumbering and slow. It plays like theUlcerated Tree Spirits.
It will growthorn-like furon its back when injured by half of its HP.

Furnace Golems are large enemies that resemble vaguely humanoid fire pits that can be easily spotted from a distance. Usual areas to find them in are large, open areas such asShadow Keep,Charo's Hidden Grave, andScorched Ruins. When defeated, they drop a unique crystal tear as well as a Furnace Visage. They're made up of branches and metal with a face plate on the front of the basket that somewhat resembles a hornsent, as well as two faces on the upper parts of its legs that resembleFire Giants. Their entire body is perpetually on fire but they can cause certain parts to burn more intensely to attack as well as attack from range using a variety of fireball attacks.
Furnace Golem,焼炉のゴーレム(Shōro no Gōremu), is an enemy inElden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree.
Furnace Golems are giant autonomous constructs made from metal branches and rods. They once spread a great inferno wherever they went, acting as weapons of mass destruction and instruments of unfathomable torture, gathering the countless, still-living bodies of man and beasts alike and added them to their ever growing collection of burning corpses. The charred human remains that are seen within are visibly locked in poses of terror and despair. Many of them reaching far outside the bars of their prison in a desperate, yet hopeless attempt to escape.
Their flames could burn away both body and soul,[1]and thus, on hismother'swishes, were used byMessmer the Impalerto cleanse the tower folk by fire,[2][3]in aCrusadewithout Grace or honor.[4]
As they were built specifically to mock and torment members of thehornsent culture, they are decorated with visages offire giantsand thefell god of firethat haunts their many sagas.[5]The mask depicting the fell god is derisively surrounded by curled horns, artifacts that which the hornsent revere most.[6]
The scattered sap of the Scadutree pools deep within the furnace golems, wherecrystal tearsare formed slowly over the ages.[7]Each Furnace Golem defeated will drop a tear that can be mixed in theFlask of Wondrous Physick.
The most common type of Furnace Golem that can be found throughout therealm of shadow. Its exposed legs allows one to deal damage to it with conventional melee attacks. All furnace golems are vulnerable toHefty Fire PotsandHefty Furnace Potsif the pots are thrown into the opening at the top of the golem, the latter of which is the more damaging variant of the two.[8]
Two of these golems can be found in theCastle Watering Hole. Where one of them, in its complete dormancy, will be blocking the entrance to theRuins of Unte. To gain access to the ruins and eventually fell this golem, then the player needs to re-awaken it with aHefty Furnace Pot, thrown into its cold, flameless basket.
Furnace golem with armored leg-bracers. Conventional melee attacks will not work on them. Players must instead find high-ground near said golem and try to throw in eitherHefty Fire PotsorHefty Furnace Potsinto its basket in order to deal damage.
The tactic of engaging the golem head-on and break its legs with repeated melee attacks.
While hitting either of its legs, it's useful to be keep the other leg in view to better identify which attack is about to come out next, so that it may be avoided accordingly. Once both legs have been broken, the golem will begin to collapse and fall face-first down on the ground, where it will persist for a very long time. Allowing for several, risk-free additional attacks and a severely-damaging critical attack to it's face. While the basket-opening at the top of the construct is easily accessible from ground-level while its knocked over, the furnace golem has near complete immunity to damage from either variant of hefty pots while in this state. However, this immunity ends immediately after performing a critical attack. So the player still has a chance to throw in a hefty pot for additional heavy damage before its able to stand up again.
Its shockwave attacks can be easily dodged by jumping (especially with Torrent's double-jump). If the golem is about to use its eruption attack, then its wise to run away and gain distance withTorrentand then get back into melee range again once the attack finishes. Do keep note that gaining too much distance for too long may trigger the golem to use its eruption attack again.
The tactic of locating nearby high-ground so that one may throw several hefty pots into the golem from above.
While only the armored variants force the player to use this method, this tactic is still applicable to every single furnace golem that can be found and is the fastest and easiest way to take out furnace golems bar none, as it does not require any stat-investment or weapon upgrades of any kind. The only things needed, are efficient resource-gathering for the required crafting materials and passable spacial awareness.
Note that it'll take about five to sevenHefty Fire Potsor two to fourHefty Furnace Potsto defeat furnace golems with this method.

Closest Site of Grace:Darklight Catacombs
From theDarklight CatacombsSite of Grace, continue straight into the dark tunnels and take the first right turn down the stairs. Once you've made your way to the bottom, go through the archway directly next to the stairs and pull the lever to light up the area. Head back to the archway directly in front of the end of the stairs and continue going down. Follow the path to the hall that you've lit up and at the end, there should be a stone lift, make your way down and continue along the path again. Carefully make your way down the stairs and down the ladders. Continue along the path down the stairs to reach another stone lift, take the lift down, and head out the archway. Continue making your way down the ladder at the straight end of the path is another lever, pull it to light up the area. Turn around and take the stairs down on the left, continue down the stairs on the right, and take another stone lift down. Once you reach the bottom, head out the archway and through the mist to find Jori, Elder Inquisitor. [Map Link] [Video Link]

The Best Tips for Jori, Elder Inquisitor:
Recommended summons:Mimic Tear,Demi-Human Swordsman Yosh
Recommended talismans:Golden Braid,Great-Jar's Arsenal
Other items:Windy Crystal Tear,Opaline Hardtear,Rakshasa Set
As the fight contains a large pool of water, utilizing Lightning weapons and spells can be helpful.
Jori, Elder Inquisitorcan be found guarding the entrance to theAbyssal Woods, fought at the end of the Darklight Catacombs. From the Site of Grace, make your way through the catacombs and through the mist to the boss' arena. This boss doesn't move fast at all and dealsPiercing Damageandholy damage. Jori will cast spells most of the time unless you are fighting at close-range, then they will start to use their staff-spear to attack you.
Jori will raise their staff and it will glow and cast out multipleholy crescents that will home in on you, this can be indicated by the small glow on the tip of the staff. You will need to dodge forward if you want to gain up to him or sideways and use the environment to block the spells so you can avoid them overall. Another spell isGolden Arcs, this is where they raise the staff but send out only three crescents in the direction of a cone towards you, this attack can be telegraphed when he slowly swings his staff from one side to the other when casting the spell. You can easily dodge to the sides to avoid it or forward if you want to get closer to him. Their next spell attack isGiant Golden Arc, which sends out a much larger crescent toward you, this attack can be telegraphed when they swing their staff towards themself to send out the spell. You can perform a perfectly timed dodge roll forward to avoid receiving damage. Jori's last spell attack isSpira, they can summon glowing spirals from the ground where you're standing that will deal damage, this attack can be telegraphed when Jori holds their staff up with both hands. You will have to keep running or dodging away from these circles to avoid receiving damage.
The rest of their attack include summoning other Inquisitors to help them in combat. During this period, you may take cover behindgravestones, especially when you see the spinning Fat Inquisitor coming up your way. These structures will cover you from their spells, and allow you to lure the summons to your side. You can take out the summons first, especially the Fat Inquisitor, and then, you can focus on Jori afterward.
Jori has a few melee attacks they perform with the staff, one of which is a simple swing; they will raise the staff and then perform a sweep. This attack can be telegraphed when they turn their body to the right, exposing their back. You will need to time your dodge to the right to avoid receiving damage as well as attacking them. Their next melee attack is Staff Stab, this attack can be indicated when they bring the staff back while facing you before thrusting. You can dodge to either side to avoid this attack and attack when you can. Once Jori, Elder Inquisitor is defeated, they will drop 260,000 Runes and aBarbed Staff-Spear.
If you keep your distance, they'll stay back. With enough room, all of their ranged attacks are not difficult to roll through or run from. The gravestones and trees will block the projectiles.
For ranged, the summons are the real difficulty. You could simply ignore them, but it is a test of patience to keep clearing them out just for another group to be summoned. Spirit Ashes is very helpful for drawing attention away.
Originally, Jori was planned to be a boss with their own Remembrance, fighting alongside a Fat Inquisitor.
Jori, Elder Inquisitoris an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree, found at the bottom of theDarklight Catacombs. This is an optional boss, but he must be defeated to access theAbyssal Woods.
One of the hornsentinquisitors, who are tasked with torture[1]and questioning.[2]
Due to his name, it can be inferred he is an inquisitor with greater power an authority than the others, and he is capable of summoning phantom inquisitors at will.
He is seemingly tasked with guarding theAbyssal Woodsthat are filled with the influence of theFlame of Frenzy, whose use was forbid by the hornsent.[3]The inquisitors impaled Midra with theGreatsword of Damnationfor trespassing this law.[4]

Thedefensenumbers are compared to the incoming attack power to determine how much to scale down the damage. The higher the ratio, the more damage comes through.
Thenegationnumbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Recommended Ashes of War:Flame of the Redmanes
Recommended skills:Golden Crux,Taker's Flames,Wave of Gold
Recommended talismans:Fire Scorpion Charm,Ritual Sword Talisman,Shard of Alexander

Rakshasa is a samurai humanoid boss in Elden Ring who wields a great katana and wears scarlet red armor. This boss can land attacks that cause heavy damage and can follow up with additional slashing attacks. To successfully defeat Rakshasa, you’ll need to time your attacks carefully. Recklessly rushing in can lead to instant death, as she can easily follow up her attacks with more strikes. Fortunately, her attacks are somewhat predictable.
When Rakshasa prepares to slash, she often backs up slightly before executing the attack. This gives you a brief moment to anticipate and dodge. Additionally, when she jumps into the air to performLeaping Slash, you can usually counter this move by attacking her mid-air. This tactic can interrupt his attack and give you an advantage.
During close-range combat, it’s crucial to retreat occasionally and adapt a defensive stance. Rakshasa can almost always counter with her own attacks unless you stagger her first. Keeping a balance between offense and defense is key. Make sure to land your hits when you see an opening but be ready to dodge and retreat to avoid her counterattacks. She can do the Double Slash move where she makes a double slash with her katana to damage you. You can counter this by rolling to the left or right to evade. Alternatively. you can also parry the first hit to stop Rakshasa from doing this attack. The next move is aKatana Thrust, which is another move that can be parried.
Watch her movements closely, anticipate her attacks, and strike when the moment is right. By maintaining a balance between aggression and defense, you can overcome this boss. Rakshasa has hyper armor during all of her attacks, making it impossible to stagger with light attacks. This makes her kind of a difficult boss to deal with, as the window to attack her are pretty tight due to her having a fast attack interval.
Rakshasais an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. She is encountered at theEastern Nameless Mausoleum.
Rakshasa is located in the Eastern Nameless Mausoleum, within theRecluses' Riverarea ofScadu Altus. The Mausoleum is located near a river bank.
Rakshasa is a vicious and frightening warrior, who only cares to "cut down and devour" her victims without repose.
Rakshasa wears her eponymous armor set; a steel suit of armor drenched in the blood of her victims.[1]She also wields a largegreat katana, her main weapon of choice for cutting down her victims like weeds[2]and devouring all those who challenge her.
