The Best Tips for Ancient Dragon Senessax:
Recommended Summons:Black Knife Tiche,Mimic Tear Ashes
Recommended Spells:Rotten Breath,Ekzykes's Decay
Avoid fighting in the pool of water, as it will further increase the range from Senessax's attacks.
As an ancient dragon, Senessax boasts high damage absorption. The battle begins with the dragon waking from its sleep and immediately performingAncient Dragons' Lightning Strike. Senessax will then take to the skies to launch aFire Breath. You must evade this by rolling, as a direct hit can deplete 90% of your health or kill you instantly. This attack has a wide AoE so you will need to spam roll multiple times to either direction (left or right).
One of the most accessible parts of the dragon to target is its feet. Since the dragon will be on the ground most of the time, you’ll have opportunities to strike its legs during combat. On the ground, Senessax relies onLightning SlamsandSweeps. These attacks are powerful but avoidable. When you see the dragon raising its arms, immediately switch to defense and roll back as far as you can. Its lightning melee attacks have a wide damage area, making it crucial to maintain distance. Due to the size of its attack, you will roll twice for the lightning stomps and the swings can be avoided by rolling backwards.
After the dragon launches an attack and misses, observe its movements closely. If it doesn't seem to attack again soon, take the opportunity to strike its legs and deal heavy damage. Be aware that when the dragon feels pressured by your attacks, it will often use its wings to blow you away, creating distance between you. One strategy that you can use against Ancient Dragon Senessax is to rideTorrentto go in and out of the battle. You can utilize Torrent to easily get out of the boss's reach whenever it attacks, then punish it when it is your turn to attack. You can also avoid Senessax's fire breath when riding Torrent as you are fast enough to outrun the flames. When attacking Senessax while riding Torrent, you should always go for its legs so you will be out of harm's way when you're attacking.
One of the moves that the Ancient Dragon Senessax does isAncient Dragons' Lightning Spearwhere you see it raise its arms to conjure a lightning bolt, then, it will stab the ground with it to create a lightning AoE damage. This move will have a variation when the boss' health drops to 50%; it will make the same move for the second time after a slight delay. To dodge this move, start by jumping twice while riding Torrent, or you can also do a jump with your character.
Another attack that is worth mentioning isWingbeat, which is a common move that the boss makes where it flaps both wings to create a wind that will blow you away. This move creates a distance between the two of you and can stagger you when it connects. To avoid this attack, spam roll backwards until you get out of the AoE.
To win the fight against Ancient Dragon Senessax, you need to time your attacks and be patient. Rushing in can lead to immediate death since almost all its attacks are very powerful. Regularly switch between defense and offense, evading more than attacking. Patience is critical; wait for the right moments to attack, and gradually, you’ll lower its health.
Ancient Dragonis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
The Ancient Dragons ruled in the prehistoric era before theErdtree.[1]They wielded red lightning as a weapon[2], and had scales made of sharp, pointed gravel stones.[3]They were ruled over byDragonlord Placidusax, said to have beenElden Lordin the time before the Erdtree[4], from the royal city ofFarum Azula[5], and it is said that they would protect their lord as a wall of living rock.[6]
Ancient Dragons have light grey bodies resembling stone. They possess four legs, as well as four wings inlayed with gold, distinguishing them from theirlesser descendants. They have short, flat muzzles, orange-yellow eyes, and wispy grey hairs along their backs. They can breathe fire like many of their descendants, however they also possess the ability to wield red lightning, which often manifests in the form of spears and glaives.
During the reign ofQueen Marika the Eternal, the Ancient Dragon Gransax wrought havoc onLeyndell, Royal Capital, the only time in recorded history that Leyndell's walls have fallen.[7]This marked the dawn of the war against the Dragons, during which the Tree Sentinels clad themselves in armor resembling the bodies of the Dragons in order to protect the Erdtree.[8]During this conflictGodwyn the Goldenfought to the last against the Ancient DragonFortissax.[9]Godwyn defeated Fortissax, however he befriended his fallen foe, ending the conflict and giving rise to the capital's Ancient Dragon Cult.[10]Worship of the Ancient Dragons does not conflict with faith in the Erdtree, as the Dragons' lightning is imbued with gold, and as such the Cult was permitted within Leyndell.[11]
Ancient Dragons are greatly resistant toStancedamage. In addition to their base 120 Stance health, they only take 20% Stance damage (effectively giving them 600 Stance health against those hits) from hits against everything except for their heads, though their heads at least take doubled Stance damage compared to the rest of their body (effectively giving them 300 Stance health against those hits). Though their Stance health won't refill unless they haven't taken Stance damage for a fairly lengthy 9.231 seconds, this, in addition to how hard their heads can be to hit, make them sturdy foes.

Lansseax, the sister of Fortissax, is said to have taken the form of a human priestess in order to commune with the knights of the Ancient Dragon Cult.[12]Her most beloved knight wasVykethe dragonspear[13], a Tarnished knight of theRoundtable Hold, who was later scourged by the frenzied flame.[14]
Lansseax is first encountered near the Abandoned Coffin Site of Grace, near the entrance to Altus Plateau from theRuin-Strewn Precipice. After sustaining enough damage, she will fly away. She can later be encountered on a hill just south-west of the Rampartside Path Site of Grace in the east of Altus Plateau, where she can be defeated for good.

Ghostflame Dragonis aField BossinElden Ring. Ghostflame Dragon is a massive dragon with withered wings and exposed bones. This boss is found throughout the Lands of Shadow. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring: Shadow of the Erdtree.
Other bosses with the same basic attacks areFlying Dragon Agheel,Flying Dragon Greyll,Glintstone Dragon Smarag,Glintstone Dragon Adula,Decaying Ekzykes,Borealis the Freezing Fog, andJagged Peak Drake.Lesser DragonandGlintstone Dragonare normal enemies with the same basic attacks.

The Ghostflame Dragon is a formidable boss in Elden Ring, it's similar to theFlying Dragon Agheeland other dragons but with unique wings that make it less prone to flight. Despite its limited aerial capability, it can still fly occasionally, so remain alert. As a melee character, your strategy should focus on agility and timing.
When the fight begins, the Ghostflame Dragon will likely start with aGhostflame Breathattack, which does frostbite damage. Watch for the dragon to wave its head downward as a sign that it’s about to unleash this attack. Due to its slow movements, this attack is relatively easy to predict and avoid. Use your Greatshield to block physical attacks, but rely on your agility to dodge its more powerful attacks. If you're not using a shield, you can roll in either direction (left or right).
The dragon’s legs are its weakest points, so prioritize attacking them whenever you see an opening. Stay close to its legs to minimize the risk of being hit by its more powerful attacks. Be observant of its movements and when the dragon raises its legs, back up and move out of the way to avoid being stomped. The dragon will also perform a ground smash after taking flight, so be prepared to dodge this attack as well. When you see the dragon's head, you can also try to do a jump attack if you can to apply an increased stance damage to it. If you knock it down, make sure to run to its head so you can deal a critical hit.
At mid-range, the Ghostflame Dragon will use aDouble Chomp attack, thrusting its jaws towards you. This move is also predictable due to the dragon’s slow overall movement. Stay agile and keep your Greatshield ready to block when necessary. At about 50% health, this boss will do a massive Ghostflame AoE attack. You will know this move when you see it stand up and its chest is burning with Ghostflame. To dodge this, keep running in the opposite direction until the animation ends. The AoE size does cover a lot of space so running is your only option to dodge here.
The Ghostflame Dragon utilizes Ghostflame strikes that can inflict frostbite, so ensure you have remedies for this status effect. Its slow movements make it a mid-difficulty boss, as its attacks are generally easy to read and anticipate. The ultimate key to defeating this dragon is to observe its movements carefully and dodge when needed. Exploit its weak points by attacking its legs, and use your Greatshield strategically to block its physical attacks while remaining agile to avoid the more dangerous moves. Another thing to note is that this boss is weak toHolyandStrike Damage; make sure to check the recommended weapon, spells, and skills to help you out in this fight.

Bell Bearing Hunteris a recurringField BossinElden Ring. He is a hunter of shopkeepers who only appears at night and features long-distance melee attacks. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring.
He will appear only at night, so if you don't see him, make sure to rest again at the nearby Site of Grace after passing time to nightfall.
SeeElemer of the Briarfor the Great Enemy version of this boss. Defeating the real Elemer will not prevent the Bell Bearing Hunters from appearing, however. Despite his fearsome reputation, the Bell Bearing Hunter cannot permanently kill merchants.

If you can climb on nearby scenery and get above the Bell Bearing Hunter's head, none of his attacks can hit you. Use spells likeNight Maiden's Mistthat can hit through structures to damage him. Even if it seems like he's going out of range, you can simply wait and he will be back in a moment.

Hit him enough times to stance break him, perform a critical and then heal while he is getting up. You will still need enough health to tank his hits and enough damage to kill him before you run out of flasks.

Elemer of the Briaris a reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Elemer of the Briar, also known as theBell Bearing Hunter, originally hailed fromEochaid, a land of proudly solitary ascetics.[1]He wears iron armor wrapped in iron thorns, which are a mark of the guilty and of those sentenced to death.[2]He was slated for execution at theShaded Castle, home of the family of House Marais, however he evaded death by snatching the sword from the site of his looming execution and furnished it with battle skills from his homeland.[3]He gained the moniker "Bell Bearing Hunter" by killing numerous merchants and instructors[4], and taking their Bell Bearings.
Elemer can be encountered in the Castellan's Hall of the Shaded Castle, the site of his failed execution. He can also appear in various locations throughout theLands Between, typically in places where merchants can be found.
The Bell-Bearing Hunter will only appear when resting at night; to make him reappear after being defeated yourself, rest at the grace and set the time to night and then rest again.

Elemer is encountered in the hall at the top of the Shaded Castle. He can channel energy through his sword, allowing him to send it towards the player and control it at a distance, or fire a red beam by rotating it quickly.
The Bell Bearing Hunter appears at night, in the Hermit Merchant's Shack in theCapital Outskirts. TheHermit Merchant (Capital Outskirts)will disappear for the duration of the fight, but will reappear if the player dies or if they defeat the boss.

The normal enemy form isLesser Sanguine Noble. The invader NPC who uses its equipment isSanguine Noble (NPC).
Known to strike from pools of blood, these assassins are missionaries come to share the gospel of accursed blood.
In the cellar ofWritheblood Ruins. [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
For melee users, be wary as the Sanguine Noble's swings are very fast, so it's recommended that you use a fast one-hand weapon like a straight sword or an axe. Every single type of attack this boss does stacks bleed so it's best that you bringStanching Boluses. Do not rush this boss and be careful with its string of stabs and slashes. Also be wary of its stance where you see the dagger on its left hand being lifted, it means it's ready to parry your incoming attacks. Do not engage in melee when you see this stance, as it will most likely parry you successfully once you try to attack. A successful parry on you will get you stabbed and also build-up your bleed meter very quickly.
For magic and ranged users, it's recommended that you equip a heavy hitting spell/incantation or weapon for ranged attacks to quickly finish the Sanguine Noble. Just be careful with the blood puddles and the dagger throw as those are also the boss' ranged options. You should also look out for the leaping thrust where it leaps forward and thrusts its sword, this move quickly closes the gap when you're trying to create distance or when you're far away from the boss for too long.

The Best Tips for Demi-Human Queen Maggie:
When dealing attacks and running within range, be aware of the rocky terrain so you don't get stuck for one of its counter attacks. It would be more beneficial for this strategy if you could lead her to flatter ground, if not just be aware of the rocks in the area. The boss has lot of similar action movesets. Basic slam sets with either her hand or staff can be avoided by rolling forward which will also put you in a better position for you next attack. If remaining in close range, she will rarely use her magic attacks. Try as much as possible to stay close to her to deal melee attack damage. A lot of her attacks will also only affect mid range but can be avoided when you stay close. Try to always circle behind her. If too close be ready to quickly roll back for her closer range smash attacks.
With longer range, she has a limited set of magic attacks. These spells she uses are basic glinstone projectile spells and can be easily avoided as soon as they are casted and you see the direction they are heading. If using magic, just be cautious because it can enrage her. You can also choose to use the same type against her, theGlintstone Shard. When choosing this method, make sure you keep circling around her and keep moving so she won't be able to target you as easily.
According to theDemi-Human Queen’s Staff, the Academy gave it to the queen in order to broker peace, which could explain the presence of the many Sorcerers.
Glintstone staff styled as a scepter. A gift once given to the demi-humans to foster peace, it can be wielded even by those of low intelligence.
Demi-Human Queen Maggieis an optionalbossinELDEN RING(2022). She is encountered at theHermit VillageonMt. Gelmir.
A demi-human queen residing in theHermit VillageonMt. Gelmir. She is surrounded by otherdemi-humansas well asGlintstone Sorcerers. She guards the resting spot ofPrimeval Sorcerer Azur.
Demi-Human Queens tower over the averageDemi-Human. They possess long, lanky limbs and canine features, and wear crowns and tattered capes. The staves they wield, which are styled as sceptres, were given to the Demi-Humans to foster peace, but are sneered at by fools at the Academy.[1]

name: Demi-Human Queen Gilika | Elden Ring Wiki
Demi-Human Queen Gilikais aField BossinElden Ring. Demi-Human Queen Gilika is a largeDemi-Humanthat wields a magical staff and is found inAltus Plateau. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring.
SeeDemi-Human Queen Margot,Demi-Human Queen Maggie, andDemi-Human Queen Mariggafor other variants of this boss.Demi-Human Queenis the normal enemy form.
Heading north from theAltus PlateauSite of Grace, intoLux Ruins. The entrance to the basement is towards the northwest end of the ruins:
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
The Best Tips for Demi-human Queen Gilika:
This boss can receive a ton of damage with aggressive attacks and has a lot of windows and opportunities to deal damage to make the fight fly by quickly. For a faster defeat, players can choose to use Spirit Summons, however this isn't necessary. She can be staggered very easily and will pause to cover her face, giving you a longer opportunity to deal more hits and keep her from her attack sequences. Along with this, her poise can be broken. Continue with these attacks while dodge or blocking her lunges until she is defeated.
Use any heavy physical damage Spell such as Rock Sling to keep her staggered and break her poise. To have an even smoother,  quick encounter, use Spirit summons to double attacks and have almost the the entire fight open to your magic or ranged attack as she focuses on the summon. Continue dealing attacks and moving back to quickly defeat this boss.
Glintstone staff styled as a scepter. A gift once given to the demi-humans to foster peace, it can be wielded even by those of low intelligence.Sneered at by fools in the academy.

You will be led to an open field of blue flowers and a waterfall, pass the waterfall, and continue northwest to eventually reach the shore, you will find the Boss seated next to what looks like a shipwreck.[Map Link]

The Best Tips for Demi-Human Queen Marigga:
Other items:Opaline Bubbletear,Opaline Hardtear
TheDemi-Human Queen Mariggacan be found in Cerulean Coast, by following the narrow path east from Cerulean Coast West - Site of Grace. It mostly performs magic damage attacks from a distance and standard damage attacks during close-range combat.
She can inflict damage by using herspells. TheDemi-Human Queen Mariggawill shoot out a projectile in your direction, this can be indicated when she raises her staff and the staff tip will shine bright blue before shooting out the projectile. There are 2 types of spells:Glintstone PebbleandCrystal Burst. Since the projectile shoots straight to you, it is recommended to dodge toward the sides or even forward to gain up to her (this applies to both spells).
TheDemi-Human Queen Marigga's close combat attack is herStaff Stab. She will raise her arm with her staff and then direct it forward and stab the ground with the staff tip, this can be indicated when she raises her staff, making it go horizontal above her before stabbing. Since this is another attack directed straight at you, perform a dodge roll toward the sides or forward to perform heavy attacks to break her stance. The next move that she can make is theFist Slam, this is a move that she does with her left arm where she pounds the ground when you're close to her. Then, finally, she also has theSwing and Stab. This is her fast move with the staff where she will start with a swing and stab to the right, and then, she will swing back. To counter this attack, all you need to do is to roll backward for the first swing, and then forward (slightly to the right).
Once you break her stance, you will be able to deal a lot more damage and eventually defeat her. TheDemi-Human Queen Mariggawill drop 100,000 Runes and theStar-Lined Swordupon defeat. This boss doesn't have a lot of HP and shouldn't take long to defeat her.
On NG, Demi-Human Queen Marigga is one of the easiest bosses in the game, dying in only a few attacks. She only gets slightly more challenging in NG+ cycles. If you are having trouble with this boss, consider bringingEkzykes's Decayto apply rot at a safe distance. Equip your best ranged spells, and be sure to clear out the smaller demi-humans before taking on the boss directly.
Sword encrusted with a line of stars fashioned from small pieces of crude glintstone. Weapon of the demi-human swordsmen. When bestowed with this weapon by their queen, the swordsmen swear to find the truth that lies at the end of the procession of stars.
Demi-Human Queen Mariggais an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. She is encountered on theCerulean Coast.
Drops theStar-Lined Sword, which implies she bestowed this weapon to the Demi-human swordsmen who swore to find the truth that lies at the end of the procession of stars.[1]
Demi-Human Swordmaster Onzerealized that only ruin awaited at the end of the procession of stars, and imprisoned himself in order to forestall it.[2]

Erdtree Burial Watchdogsare FieldBossesinElden Ring. These catlike hounds guard catacombs throughout the Lands Between, wielding swords and staves as well as elemental magic. These are optional bosses, meaning players don't need to defeat them in order to advance.
TheLesser Burial Watchdogis the normal enemy form of this boss.
The Watchdogs, battered and broken over their lengthy tenure, rule the catacombs and are even said to command the imps.

Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs.
The Best Tips for Erdtree Burial Watchdog:
Kaiden Sellsword Ashesmake early Watchdog fights a breeze.
If you hit a Watchdog with severalCrystal Darts, it will go berserk and attack the closest thing, whether it be friend or foe. This can force it to focus on your summons while you attack it at range, but its most useful for forcing the Watchdog inImpaler's Catacombsto fight itsImpsor the Watchdogs inMinor Erdtree Catacombsto fight one another.
For melee users, the best way to win this fight is to bait its attacks. Try dodge rolling to its side after a strike, get a few hits in, then dodge away. Some of its attacks covers a wide range, so having a good shield is also handy, but avoid guarding against the Levitating attacks since they can hit over a shield. If you end up behind the Watchdog, beware of its Tail Slam attack that can still hit you.
Jump Attacks:Jumping is effective for dodging both the Levitating and Spinning Swipe attacks. Jump to dodge and then do a jumping attack to build upStancedamage and get incritical hits.
Parries:Since their attacks are well-telegraphed, they can beparriedwith relative ease.
This fight is considerably easier for ranged and magic users since all you need to do is keep your distance. You may have to roll or jump away several times during the Levitating attacks, since it likes to do this many times in a row, but eventually it will stop and switch to more easily punishable attacks.
Glintstone PebbleandLightning Spearare excellent spells for these fights. Spells that can stun them such asRock Slingcan also help.
Formerly calledBurial Tree Watchdogsin the Closed Network Test.
Erdtree Burial Watchdogis an enemy and reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Erdtree Burial Watchdogs are living statues resembling beasts with hunched bodies and long, cat-like tails. Thesegolemsare the protectors of catacombs where Erdtree burial took place, and are said to command theImps.[1]
If struck by aCrystal Dart, they will enter a maddened state and attack enemies around them.

Miranda the Blighted Bloomis a FieldBossinElden Ring. This giant flower releases clouds of poisonous pollen into the air. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance.
TheGiant Miranda Sproutis the normal enemy form of this boss. Another Miranda boss appears in theOmenkiller and MirandaFlower duo fight.
Miranda, maiden of the Flower Crucible is said to have been the very first of this breed.
Closest Site of Grace:Tombsward Catacombs
This fight features severalMiranda Sproutsas well, but only the Blighted Bloom needs to be defeated to win
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
The Best Tips for Miranda the Blighted Bloom:
Use aTorchto light the Miranda on fire and interrupt most of its attacks
Be aggressive: you won't be able to avoid its poison cloud in such close quarters, so you'll need to kill it before the poison kills you. Alternate hits with aTorchto interrupt its attacks and a normal melee weapon to deal damage while it's recovering. If you deal damage quickly enough, you can largely ignore theMiranda Sprouts.
Use spells that prioritize damage over casting speed: it's hard to avoid being poisoned, but the flower's attacks are mostly slow and unable to interrupt you. InflictFire Damageif possible—not only is the Miranda quite weak to it, it can interrupt its attacks. Just be sure to get out of the way when its Rain of Light attack starts charging up.
Name changed to “Miranda Blossom” in an unknown patch.

name: Tibia Mariner | Elden Ring Wiki
Tibia Marineris aField BossinElden Ring. These hunched skeleton dress in lace and ride a ghostly boat. It steers its vessel and attacks the player with a large horn and the aid of undeadSkeletons. They are optional bosses, as players don't need to defeat them in order to advance inElden Ring.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Stay onTorrentthroughout the battle to more easily follow the Tibia Mariner when it teleports.
Use a spirit ash that can help you distract theSkeletons, like theLone Wolf Ashes.
Yee Haw:Stay mounted onTorrent, run in for a few hits, then run away again. TheSkeletonsare slow enough that you won't need to worry about them, and the Tibia Mariner's attacks are slow enough that you probably won't get hit often.
Slow and Steady:If you're fighting on foot, focus on damaging the Tibia Mariner itself and try to avoid getting hit by the Skeletons. Hit the boss a few times and then dodge out of the way when it starts attacking. Keep repeating this, staying to its side or behind it if you can. The Crashing Wave attack will kill Skeletons as well, which can help control the crowd.
Stay on horseback and keep back when attacking. The Tibia Mariner moves slowly and doesn't have any way to punish ranged attacks other than its allies, which move slowly in their own right as well. If they start crowding you, run to the other side of the boss and attack from there.
They always dropDeathroot, which signifies their control overThose Who Live in Death.
They also occasionally summon aGiant Skeleton (Spirit).

Tibia Marinersare optionalbossesinELDEN RING(2022).
Mariners are grave keepers who ferry lost souls across a sea in thespirit world.[1][2][3][4]They navigate their spectral vessels through ghostly waters withalpine hornsthat, when blown, summonThose Who Live in Death.[5]Their movement is not restricted to water when they appear in theLands Between.
The Tibia Mariners were the first of all grave keepers in theLands Between.[6]They beckonThose Lost in Deathby blowing into their hollow oars.[5][7]They have guided the dead to theGravesite Plainfor an eternity,[3]unbothered by their bones having long since crumbled to dust.[1]
The ancient mariners themselves were laid to rest amongst the crimson fields ofCharo's Hidden Grave.[8]Their secrets were inherited by future generations ofgrave keepers,[9]who used theirskullsascatalystsforsummoningwanderingspirits.[10]Their boats, or recreations of them, were prominently displayed in theShadow Keep'sChurch District. The importance of the oarsmen was recognized even amongst the living.
The Tibia Mariners were suppressed when theRune of Deathwas removed from theElden Ring.[5]In their absence, those withoutMarika'sGracewho met a glorious end in battle were left to wander.[11][12]The heroes of herGolden OrderreceivedErdtree Burial,[13]and had no need for the archaic ferrymen.[14]
WhenGodwyn the Goldenwas buried at the base of theErdtree, he soon transformed into the piscinePrince of Death.[15]Theblightleaked from his body and infected the great tree roots, and manifested itself asDeathrootthroughout the Lands Between.[16]The Tibia Mariners slowly resurfaced, andThose Who Live in Deathanswered their call.[5][17]
Gurranqthe Beast Clergyman chargesD, Hunter of the Dead, and theTarnishedto hunt down the Tibia Mariners and reap their Deathroot.[18]He believes he can restore the sanctity of the Golden Order by absorbing the residual fragments ofDestined Death.[19][20][21]
The seated Tibia Mariner uses analphornto paddle his incorporeal rowboat across ethereal, violet waters. His body is skeletonized, save for the wizened beard that clings to his slack mandible. A floral pattern decorates the white-laced chapel veil that rests upon his head and drapes over his bony frame. Attached to the veil are wide, golden hoops, each adorned with three large golden flower emblems inlaid with rubies. The mariner's forearms are wrapped in cloth, and several gold bracelets hang from his wrists. He wears the tattered remains of robes sewn from purple thread.
The mariner's transparent wooden rowboat shimmers with a faint purple hue. A chair is built into its deck, with a semi-circle cut into the backrest to create a depression at the top. Spiral patterns ascend its stile and backpost before transitioning into straight lines beaming upward. The backpost extends several feet higher than the chair and terminates in an upward concave arch reminiscent ofMarika's Rune. Hanging ventrally from it is a small lantern alight with a purpleghostflame.[22]The boat's exterior hull is highly decorated with intricate relief carvings. Two adjacent floral embellishments are encircled by spiral-containing rings and bound together with a sturdy knot. The gunwale trim above features a wavelength weaving over and under stars, possibly symbolic of thePrimeval Current.
The mariner will sometimes whip up a great torrent of water that carries his boat high into the air. When it reaches it apex, he extends his arm, and a bright red light emanates from a jewel in his palm. This light is said to beckon the lostspiritsof those slain in battle.[11]
The dry and metallic moans of the mariner eerily echo upon themselves as if uttered from deep within a dungeon. When he sounds his lengthy brass horn, a single clang of metal deeply reverberates like a tolling bell. When cast, his ancient Death magic produces a haunting noise like the crashing of cymbals.[2]

area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Abductor Virgin | Elden Ring Wiki
Abductor Virgins, also known as Iron Virgins are anEnemyinElden Ring.Abductor Virginsare theBossvariant of this enemy.
Scadu Altus: Moorth Highway South, two behind theFort of Reprimand
The Iron Virgin is a large metal construct resembling a metal statue of a saintly woman cradling a small silver baby to its chest, with several snakes winding around her upper body. From its shoulders hang a pair of long, spindly arms ending in one of two deadly weapons- a pair of pendulum blades on chains, or a pair of massive circular sawblades attached to long, rigid forearms. Its "dress" features a set of doors that swing open to reveal a hollow chamber full of blood-red fog and several metal snakes coiled up around a central rod hanging from below the Virgin's torso. Six of these metal snakes form a pair of long, tentacle-like "arms", each made of three snakes wound together and ending in three-fingered "hands", with the snakes' heads forming the fingers. Instead of legs, the Iron Virgin rolls around on a spherical wheel, allowing it to move in any direction horizontally without having to turn its whole body around.
Iron Virgins can be found slowly patrolling their territory on the lookout for intruders, or simply standing still on guard. When attacking, the Iron Virgin will immediately rush over and attack their target, spinning their arms in a wide circle to cut down enemies from every direction. The sickle-wielding variety can launch their blades from far away with deadly accuracy, even leading their blade in whatever direction their target is running so as not to miss, and then pull it back via its chain. Sawblade-wielding iron virgins prefer to charge forward at their targets with sawblades spinning full-tilt, mowing down opponents like a bulldozer.
All types of Iron Virgin have a special attack using their torture chambers- when an opponent gets too close, the doors in their front swing open, the snake-arms inside unfold, and they will attempt to grab anyone who gets too close. Once ensnared, the Iron Virgin's victim will be dragged inside, the doors will shut, and they will be helplessly attacked by the metal snakes inside before being unceremoniously thrown back out, if their victim doesn't outright die while inside the torture chamber.
Abductor Virgins, which are visually indistinguishable from Iron Virgins, will teleport whoever they capture to another location far away.-In other words, the Abductor Virgin at the bottom ofRaya Lucariawill transport you toVolcano Manor, but the one inRedmane Castlewill not.
Weak toLightning Damage(Lightning Spearis especially useful for this)
Neutral toStrike Damage, low resistance to other types of damage.Lone Abductor Virgin met at lava part of Volcano Manor is immune toFire Damage
Lone Abductor Virgin met at lava part of Volcano Manor is immune toFire Damage
Can be stance-broken, but not riposted afterwards
Weak spot: Innards, exposed both after stance-break and during a charge attack.
Takes extra stance damage from lightning damage. 5 casts ofThunderboltare sufficient to stance break them, but repeated casts are unlikely to hit the innards as the head usually blocks the innards from the thunderbolt.
One full cycle ofDragon Halberdskill breaks their stance. Other full cycle targeted at their innards should be enough to eliminate them.With Dragon Halberd it is recommended to bait their ranged attack, as it gives enough time to use said skill.
With Dragon Halberd it is recommended to bait their ranged attack, as it gives enough time to use said skill.
Beware of getting face-to-face in melee range - you will take massive damage if caught by the hands in a grab attack.
The Swinging Sickle blades can and will easily pass through walls, so hiding behind a corner will do you no good. However, the Iron Virgin cannot jump, and it has difficulty attacking targets on higher ground, so the terrain can still be used to your advantage.
The one you encounter at the bottom of the lift in the Academy can be easily beaten by standing underneath the wheel of the lift. It can't reach you from there.  Beware, as dying by its grab attack will trap you in the Volcano Manor.

The one at Redmane Castle has one pendulum blade, and one sawblade, utilizing both to its advantage.

Great iron wheel lined with flesh-flaying blades. Device of torture used by Inquisitor Ghiza. As the wheel spins it causes severe pain and blood loss.
The design was adopted for use as the iconic weapon wielded by Iron Virgins.
Mt. Gelmir, which houses the Volcano Manor at its summit, is characterized by sheer cliffs and ominous skies. These qualities only became more pronounced after the Shattering.
Abductor Virginis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
Abductor Virgins are automatons affiliated with theVolcano Manor. Originally designed with the intent of capturing and transposing victims for interrogation, they can be found strewn around theLands Between. Though the majority have lost their powers of transposition, they will still attempt to fulfill their original directive if approached.
To aid in their task, Abductor Virgins have been outfitted with heavy weaponry on both arms that alter how they approach each target. When a Virgin has approached a target, they will open their chest cavity and attempt to pull them in withserpentinetendrils. Given the loss of their transposition ability, the target will be constricted instead. If they survive this, they will be spat back out.
They are weak toLightningdamage and all damage taken is greatly increased if attacked when their chest cavity is opened during a charge or attempted grab.
Caria ManorRaya Lucaria AcademyMt. GelmirCapital OutskirtsLeyndell, Royal CapitalVolcano Manor
A model with arms that end in great iron wheels, based on the device used byInquisitor Ghiza.[1]One such model lies at the bottom of the big waterwheel of Raya Lucaria, its transpostitional powers still fully intact.[2]
These variants will often use their wheels by pressing them down on the ground. When placing both wheels at their sides, they will either perform a small spin in place, or a larger spin where they gradually spiral outwards. When there is distance, the Virgin will place both wheels in front and rapidly accelerate forward. Sometimes they will stop before reaching the target and open their chest cavity in an attempt to grab them.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Raya Lucaria AcademyCaelidMt. GelmirVolcano Manor
A model with arms that end in great scythes on chains that it can extend and retract at will. Though they only have one spin attack, they will often use it to get some distance between them and their target. At the very end, they may throw their scythes at the target. This is something that they will do whenever there is sufficient distance. It is important to be careful after dodging the initial throw, as the scythe may hit when it is being retracted. This is especially true when near the Virgin, as the scythe will spin back around behind it upon return.
It's important to note that the Scythe can sometimes go through walls.

Alabaster Lordis aHumanoid CreatureinElden Ring.Alabaster Lordsare rare enemies, most commonly found in caves. Their look is that of a very tall and slim humanoid with stone skin and long hair. They wield a rather long Greatsword, as opposed to the Onyx Lords, who use curved greatswords. For the Boss variants seeOnyx Lordpage. They have aweaknessto gravity related weapons.
A race of ancients with skin of stone who were said to have risen to life when a meteor struck long ago.
You can find one of these creatures at the shores ofSouth Limgrave. It is settled under a large, arched structure, warming up to a bonfire. This Lesser Alabaster Lord dropsAsh of War: Gravitaswhen defeated. [Map Link]
One appears out of a floating purple sphere in theYelough Anix Tunnel.
One appears on the raised pillars at theLake of Rotand drops theAlabaster Lord's Swordwhen killed.

They also have a darker counterpart that wields acurved greatswordknown as theOnyx Lord.
The Alabaster Lords are a race of ancients with skin of stone who were said to have risen to life when a meteor struck long ago.
One of the Alabaster Lords became a mentor ofGeneral Radahnand taught him Gravity Magic, withCollapsing Stars,Gravity WellandRock Slingbeing three of the gravitational techniques studied by the young Radahn.

name: Battlemage Hugues | Elden Ring Wiki
Battlemage Huguesis aBossinElden Ring. Battlemage Hugues is a Haima Battlemage and is found inSellia Evergaol, in centralCaelidnorth from Sellia. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring.
Battlemageis the normal enemy form of this boss. Battlemage Hugues can be summoned as spirits for aid in battle throughBattlemage Hugues Ashes.
Hugues came from Sellia to study the Haima Conspectus at the academy, where he became a battlemage.
Haima scholars seek to quell conflict with cannon fire and the gavel, but Hugues developed a longing for it.
From theDragonbarrow WestSite of Grace, follow the crevasse east and then south. At the end of the cliffside, you'll findSellia Evergaolwhich holds Battlemage Hugues. [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
For melee users, try using a heavy or colossal weapon as the mage is easily staggered.
Try equipping theRock Slingspell for magic users.
Bring theCarian Knight's Shieldto block his many magic attacks.
Once you start the battle, walk up towards the summoning area, and quickly go behind the mage to perform a backstab. You can easily circle around the mage and continue performing backstab. If you manage to screw the rotation it's fine, wait for the mage to perform the Gavel of Haima and dodge roll through the slam, you can quickly get behind him and do a backstab, or you can just get a few swings in if you prefer that.
If you're using a colossal or heavy weapon, you'll easily stagger him with just a few swings, breaking his string of attacks. Once he's on his knees, you can then perform a crit attack.
If you are a magic and ranged user, it's best to have a shield that can highly negate magic damage like theCarian Knight's Shield, he will use the Glintstone Shard spell if you try to create some distance, so you can either time your dodge correctly to avoid the attack or block it. You can try baiting him in using some melee attacks then dodge roll away, then cast your spells/incantations or fire away some arrows.
Alternatively you can just useNight Maiden's Mist. Get the tree between you and the boss and shoot the mist over the tree. Hughes will automatically retaliate as long as he takes damage, effectively pining himself into the mist but you should be safe with the trunk acting as a shield. Reapply the mist before it ends to kill him effortlessly.
The same enemy can be encountered as aBattlemagearound various locals, like Altus Plateau and Liurnia.

Battlemageis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
Scholars of the HaimaConspectusof theAcademy of Raya Lucaria. Haima scholars are the adjudicators of the Academy,[1]who studied sorceries of cannon and gavel in order to gain the power to quell conflict.[2]Whenever war broke out and the Academy sealed its gates, the battlemages of Haima were the only scholars who dared venture outside.[3]As such, they can be found in many regions of theLands Between. The stone clubs they carry reflect their more forceful approach, allowing them to feel the impact of their blows so they do not lose sight of the true essence of battle.[4]

name: Black Knife Assassin | Elden Ring Wiki
Black Knife AssassinsareBossesinElden Ring. ThisElden Ring Black Knife Assassin Guidefeatures boss locations, tips, strategies and videos on how to defeat the Black Knife Assassins easily, as well as boss stats and lore for the Black Knife Assassins. Bosses are unique and challengingEnemiesthat can be encountered all over the Lands Between. They can drop uniqueSpirit Ashes,Weapons,Spells, and other variousItems.
The Black Knife Assassins are relentless and agile dark figures that become more fearsome and deadly the deeper you venture into The Lands Between. They were responsible for the event known as the Night of the Black Knives, where they assassinatedGodwyn the Goldenwith daggers imbued with a fragment of the Rune of Death stolen fromMaliketh, the Black Blade. These assassins are a group of women who are said to be Numen with close connections toQueen Marika.
These are optional bosses as players don't have to defeat them to advance inElden Ring. Despite being quick and hard hitters, the Black Knife Assassins are easily staggered and having Spirit Ashes to distract them can help significantly. The variant in theSage's Caveis invisible, though there are multiple methods available to pinpoint her location during the fight, the easiest of which is using theSentry's Torch. Black Knife Assassins drop theAssassin's Crimson Dagger,Assassin's Cerulean Dagger,Black Knifeprint,Concealing Veil, orBlack Knifedepending on which assassin was defeated.
Lesser Black Knife Assassinis the normal enemy form of this boss.Alecto, Black Knife Ringleaderis another variant of this boss.
The spirit of a Black Knife Assassin can be summoned for aid in battle by using theBlack Knife TicheSpirit Ashes.
The assassins that carried out the deeds of the Night of the Black Knives were all women, and rumored to be Numen who had close ties with Marika herself.

Magic Glintbladecan make this boss laughably easy, as it tends to dodge while the spell is casted, meaning that it does not dodge the projectile itself.
The Assassin can be easily staggered, and theLone Wolves Ashescan distract her, deal a lot of damage, and leave openings to land some free hits. Otherwise, use a fast weapon to keep her staggered so she can't attack you back. They also have rather low health, so it's often worthwhile to trade damage and just plan to outlast her.
The safest way to attack her is to wait for her Helmsplitter and use her recovery time to set up a backstab. You can also try parrying her, but it's not recommended as her attacks are fast and hard to predict and she tends to move around a lot.
Intelligence: Keep your distance and use ranged attacks. Cemetery Shadeis aBossinElden Ring. ThisElden Ring Cemetary Shade Guidefeatures boss locations, tips, strategies and videos on how to defeat Cemetary Shades easily, as well as boss stats and lore for the Cemetary Shades.
Cemetery Shadeis a dark and formless humanoid brandishing two sharp blades. They are found in various catacombs - theTombsward Catacombs,Black Knife Catacombs, andCaelid Catacombs. While the nature of the Cemetary Shades is largely ambiguous, the description of theMantis Bladesthey carry suggest that they are grave keepers infested with insects.
This is an optional boss, as players are not required to defeat it in order to advance inElden Ring. While they may be frail, they makes up for it with quick flurries of attacks, while also phasing in and out to strike. It may be worthwhile to bringConsumablesand/or put onEquipmentthat can alleviate the build-up ofHemorrhageas some of their attacks can inflict the status effect. Cemetary Shades dropLhutel the Headless, theTwinsage Sorcerer Ashes, orKindred of Rot Ashesdepending on which one was defeated.

UseOpaline Bubbletearbefore entering the boss arena to ensure you'll have time to to use yourSpirit Calling Bell.
Use theSwift Glintstone ShardSpell to hit it, as it can easily dodge slower sorceries.
BringStanching Bolusesto preventHemorrhage.
Blitz it Down:Cemetery Shade has extremely low health. If you've got enough damage output and the vitality to survive a few hits, you'll probably win a fight where you just trade blows until one of you dies.
Defensive Maneuvers:If you want to play defensively, equip a shield with 100% physical negation. Block its attacks andguard counterafterwards to get in damage and wear down itsStance. You can alsoparryits attacks, but the timing is difficult since they come in rapid succession. It can still inflictHemorrhagethrough a shield, so be ready to consume aStanching Bolus.
Quick Attacks:Cemetery Shade tends to teleport quickly around the arena, making it hard to hit if your cast time is slow or if you're using a ranged weapon skill like theMighty Shot. Spells that likeSwift Glintstone Shardthat can be cast quickly are helpful, as long as you avoid its projectile attacks.
Greatbows Barrage:A hit from aGreatbowwill knock Cemetery Shade down if it hits. You can ensure that it does by firing right after it teleports. It'll take enough time getting back up for you to nock another arrow and repeat the process.

Deathbirdis aField BossinElden Ring. A Deathbird is a bipedal bird with a decrepit appearance wielding a long fire poker and is found in various locations, but only at night. They share a close resemblance with theDeath Rite Birdbut cannot wield magic and are much weaker than their larger winged variants. This is an optional boss as players do not have to defeat it to advance.
The Deathbirds are graveyard fire keepers; it is said they rake out the ashen remains of the dead from their kilns.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Holy Water Potscan take advantage of its weakness toHolydamageandthe pots' inherent 400% damage bonus againstThose Who Live in Deathto do massive damage even at lowFaith
TheSacred Bladeskill is another great way for non-Faithbuilds to doHolydamage
Stay on foot rather than riding Torrent. A Deathbird can leap a great distance, and the reach on its poker is long enough to clip you even when you're running at full speed on Torrent. Even ranged players should try to stay just outside the range of its swings, and keep the flexibility to dodge out of the way when it attacks
Stay close to its hind legs, time your dodges, and get a few swings in after every attack. Don't get greedy and attack more than a few times.
O Holy Fight:Because Deathbirds are bothThose Who Live in Deathandweak toHolydamage, melee builds with highFaithwill have a particularly easy time defeating them. TheOrder's Bladeincantation is easy to get and will give your weapon a tremendous damage boost against this boss.
It's Litany:ForFaith-based magic builds,Litany of Proper Deathwill make short work of this fight. Because Deathbirds are bothThose Who Live in Deathandweak toHolydamage, it will do a whopping 1400% extra damage. Just be aware that it will only work when the Deathbird is touching the ground, so time the incantation carefully.
The Deathbirds are said to have been born from a “Twinbird,” said to be the envoy for an outer god.

name: Fallingstar Beast | Elden Ring Wiki
Fallingstar Beastis aField BossinElden Ring. This a massive quadruped is covered in crystals and is found in multiple locations. This is an optional boss as players are not required to defeat it to advance inElden Ring, but doing so will yield useful items andRunes.
Sellia Crystal Tunnel[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
AnyThrowing Potcan be used to hit its face while it charges to knock it to the ground, briefly stunning it.
Use ashes that deal elemental damage, like theTwinsage SorcererorLatenna.
UseHoarfrost Stompas an easy source of magic damage.
Almost all of its attacks do Physical damage, so bring aShieldwith 100% Physical Resistance
Play it Safe:Fallingstar Beasts have high defense, lots of health, strong attacks, and quick movement. Focus on staying alive and learning to dodge its various attacks. Try to stay two or three boss-lengths away and wait for good openings where you can get in one or two attacks, particularly on its vulnerable face. Even when it raises its head, you can often hit its face with a jump attack.
Critical Theory:When you break Fallingstar Beast'sstanceand get the opportunity for a critical hit, don't take it right away. It'll stay down for four full seconds, during which its face is totally vulnerable. Get in a couple good whacks before you do the critical hit by using heavy attacks or jump attacks to avoid triggering the crit too early.
One of the special moves that this boss can do is the Gravitas where you see it rise up onto its hind legs, then falls down with a burst of purple magic which pulls you in if you're nearby, then raises its head and summons rocky spikes out of the ground around it. This move can be dodged by sprinting away when you see it rear up, but this attack doesn't do much damage so it may be worth just trading hits. The next one is the Gravity Bolts, this is a move where its mandible glows purple lightning as lightning gathers under your feet, then lifts its head and calls a small cluster of stone spikes up where the lightning lingers. Then, the boss will repeat the move in a smaller area, then finally in a much larger area. To dodge this, you need to print to avoid the first two hits, then sprint to the edge of the area of the third hit and roll as you approach the boundary. Try to end up near the boss to get in a few hits as it recovers.
Dodge and Weave:The most important thing to do is avoid death. This is a long battle against a strong foe, so focus on learning to dodge or block its attacks and only get in your own damage during one of the Fallingstar Beast's long recovery periods. Be patient, don't get greedy, and eventually you'll take it down.
Closest Site of Grace:Sellia Crystal Tunnel
The end boss ofSellia Crystal Tunnel. [Map Link]

Fallingstar Beastis a reoccurringbossinELDEN RING(2022)and.
Fallingstar Beasts are creatures formed of shiny black rock. They have spiky tails, patches of white fur, and insect-like mandibles. They are found in craters, likely indicating that they plummeted onto theLands Betweenfrom a great distance.
The more mature Full-Grown Fallingstar Beast have greater magical abilities, able to control gravity in their vicinity and unleash great magical beams akin toComet Azur.
They can use Gravity-based abilities, much like other enemies associated with meteors and fallen stars such asAlabaster Lords,Onyx Lords, andWithered Astel. Much like those other enemies, they are also weak to gravity-based sorceries. Additionally, extraterrestrial weapons such as theWing of Asteland theAlabaster Lord's Swordandgravity imbued weaponssuch as theStarscourge GreatswordandRadahn's Speargreatarrows deal bonus damage to these foes.

On the bridge directly south of theFarum GreatbridgeSite of Grace. [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
SeeFlying Dragon Agheelfor a full boss guide
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Stand on the elevated areas overlooking the bridge and snipe Greyll from afar. Its breath attacks don't track upwards very well so you can attack safely with minimal fear of reprisal.
UseSerpentbone ArrowsorRotbone Arrowsand stand on one end of the bridge, just barely close enough so that your arrows can reach. If Greyll starts using a long-range fire attack, run away and come back once it's settled down
The dragons that escaped the scarlet rot and made nest of the plateau to Caelid's north. Thus it was named "Dragonbarrow," and none dare to enter.
Superior incantation of Dragon Communion.Channels the power of Greyoll, the Elder Dragon.An incantation of legendary status.
Transforms caster into a dragon to emit a terrible roar,reducing the attack power and defense of nearby enemies.
Greyoll was the mother of all dragons,dwarfing all who stood before her like a looming mountain.
Solidified grease made from a gravel-stone mixture. Craftable item.
Coats armament, granting an anti-dragon effect.The effect lasts only for a short time.
When the dragons were born from their ancient kin, they lost their stone scales, which can now be used to cause them mortal harm.
Dragonis an enemy and category of boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Paltry, mortal descendants of theAncient Dragons[1]who once ruled theLands Between. They did not inherit their ancestors' command over lightning, and are instead vulnerable to it.[2]They typically possess  large wings in the place of front limbs. They have lost the stone scales possessed by their ancient kin, which can now be used to cause them mortal harm.[3]
Dragons are the offspring of Greyoll, a vast Dragon who dwarfed all who stood before her.[4]Greyoll, along with some of her children, escaped theScarlet Rotby settling on the plateau in the north ofCaelid, which became known asGreyoll's Dragonbarrow.[5]However, Greyoll appears to have succumbed to the rot, and can no longer take flight.
Dragons became the prey of hunters. Their hearts in particular were sought after by those who practiced Dragon Communion, who gained overwhelming power by consuming them.[6]Those who partook in Dragon Communion would eventually becomeMagma Wyrms, cursed to crawl the earth upon their bellies.[7]
Dragons who settled in northern Caelid with their mother, Greyoll. They surround the colossal Elder Dragon, who is now too decrepit to fight.
There are six red-eyed Flying Dragons surrounding Greyoll. Greyoll will lose 20% of her health with each Dragon killed, meaning that killing five will cause Greyoll to die.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
Dragons imbued with glintstone, who roost atop the Moonlight Altar in westernLiurnia of the Lakes. They can emit glintstone breath, which inflictsmagicdamage.
These Dragons do not respawn when killed.
A Flying Dragon encountered in Agheel Lake in southern Limgrave, north-west of theDragon-Burnt Ruins. It appears by flying down from above, torching a congregation ofWandering Nobleswith dragonfire.
Nobles in the ruins around the lake, chanting Agheel's name, praying that it will burn them to ash.[8]
Bloody Finger Hunter Yurais available as a summon for this fight, after speaking to him under the ruin south of the lake.
Defeating Flying Dragon Agheel will unlockAgheel's Flame, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor twoDragon Hearts.
A devourer of sorcerers, whose body gradually became corrupted by the glintstones of those he ate.[9]Smarag is encountered near an island west of theAcademy of Raya Lucariaand north of theTemple Quarter, guarding a corpse that holds theAcademy Glintstone Key. Note that it isnotnecessary to kill this dragon to get the Academy Glintstone Key; it can be retrieved by either sneaking behind it or rushing beyond it before it's fully awakened to get at the corpse.
Smarag is able to fireGlintstone Cometshardsfrom his mouth, and can also unleash magic breath, akin to the fire breath of other Dragons.
Defeating Glintstone Dragon Smarag will unlockSmarag's Glintstone Breath, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor twoDragon Hearts.
A devourer of sorcerers, whose body became corrupted by glintstone. Adula was once bested byRanni the Witch, and subsequently swore a knightly oath to her Dark Moon.[10]
Adula is first encountered outsideRanni's Risein the Three Sisters, north ofCaria Manor. After a brief fight it disappears, only to reappear at the Moonlight Altar, outside theCathedral of Manus Celes.
Adula can use magic breath, much like Smarag, however it can also utiliseAdula's Moonblade, conjuring a magic blade in its maw mid-flight and unleashing a wave that inflictsFrostbite.
A Flying Dragon encountered on the Farum Greatbridge, on the northern peninsula of Greyoll's Dragonbarrow. Greyoll is identical to Agheel in both appearance and ability, however the bridge gives the player much less room to manoeuvre.
A massive but stationary dragon encountered inGreyoll's Dragonbarrow, just south ofFort Faroth. She is immobile, either having grown too weak to move or as a result of having fused with the surrounding rocks, but can still let loose fearsome roars to weaken her enemies.
Greyoll is known as the mother of the lesser dragon.[11]
Defeating any the six lesser dragons surrounding her will cause large amounts of damage to her, and killing them all will kill her.
Defeating Elder Dragon Greyoll will unlockGreyoll's Roar, which can be obtained at the altar in theCathedral of Dragon CommunioninCaelidfor threeDragon Hearts.
While the intended method of defeating her is by killing the surrounding lesser dragons, killing Greyoll herself directly through another method, such asBlood Loss, will also kill these smaller dragons. This method will also effectively give another 20,000 runes, making this an excellent place to use aGold-Pickled Fowl Footfor more runes early on.
A Dragon plagued by Scarlet Rot, encountered north-west of theCathedral of Dragon Communion. Also known as the Dragon Communion Revenger, Ekzykes did not forget his hatred even as he succumbed to the rot.[12]

Frenzied Duelistis aField BossinElden Ring. Frenzied Duelist is found inGaol Cave. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Take advantage of his slow recovery to backstab him repeatedly
Banished Knight Engvallcan nearly solo him with stun locks
Always Be Circling:Roll through his attacks and try to end up behind him, or if you're further away, keep back to avoid the Ball & Chain attack while circling. Go for backstabs if you can, or just land attacks opportunistically while he's recovering. His moves are slow enough thatguard counteringis particularly effective.
Ranged players should avoid standing at a medium-long range that will cause him to use his Axe Chain Swing attack, since that's particularly hard to evade. Either use short-range spells from a medium-close range, or keep far away and hit him while he jogs slowly towards you.
Grave Warden Duelistis an enemy and reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
Former gladiators who were exiled from the colosseum.[1]They wear bronze armor adorned with snakes, which are viewed as traitors to theErdtree, and as such the audiences of their duels would delight in seeing them beaten and battered.[2]
After their banishment, they became grave wardens, and can be found in catacombs. Some have been infected by theScarlet Rot.
Duelist HelmGravekeeper CloakDuelist Greaves
Duelists that wield colossal axes, with heavy iron balls attached using iron chains.
There is a shadowy Grave Warden Duelist in the Sainted Hero's Grave, who can only be defeated if they are lured into a circle of light.

Rotten Duelist HelmRotten Duelist Greaves
Axe-wielding Duelists who have been corrupted by Scarlet Rot, which has stained their armor red. Their helms are crowned with many snakes, and when they grab a foe the bronze snake coiled around their arms will come alive and bite them, inflicting Scarlet Rot. One can be found in the Consecrated Snowfield, north ofOrdina, Liturgical Town.
Hammer-wielding Duelists who have been corrupted by Scarlet Rot, which has stained their armor red. Their helms are crowned with many snakes, and when they grab a foe the bronze snake coiled around their arms will come alive and bite them, inflicting Scarlet Rot. One can be found in the Consecrated Snowfield, west of the Consecrated Snowfield Site of Grace.

name: Guardian Golem | Elden Ring Wiki
Guardian Golemis aBossinElden Ring. Guardian Golem is a towering construct that wields a large axe inHighroad Cave. This is an optional boss as players are not required to defeat it to advance inElden Ring.
Golemis the normal enemy form of this boss.
One of the many constructs found across the Lands Between. It wields a large halberd to attack, along with being able to breath fire on anything below it.
Deep within theHighroad Cavein the far north ofLimgrave. [Map Link]
Can be poise broken, allowing for acritical hit
Critical hits deal massive damage to Guardian Golem
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs.
Stay just behind its legs. Most of its attacks aim forward or just in front of its feet.
Charge and Crit:Two charged heavy attacks from most weapons are enough to stagger Guardian Golem. Once it falls to the ground, you have a chance a chance for acritical hiton its chest which will do a massive amount of damage. It's slow enough that you should be able to get in a charged attack after each successful evasion, so stay close to its ankles and roll through its melee attacks. Be careful of Pool of Fire, though, and run away when you see him lean towards the ground.
Ankle Biter:Guardian Golem is slow and has limited ranged attacks, so you may have an easier time than a melee user. As soon as you enter the arena, immediately begin shooting at its ankles while trying to keep your distance. The golem will eventually topple, at which point you can either go for acritical hitwith a melee weapon or just use the downtime to do as much damage as you can without fear of counterattacks.

Guardian Golemis anenemyinELDEN RING(2022).
Golems are giant stone guardians hailing from a civilization now gone to ruin.[1]They are said to have been made by a golem crafter, using an impure crystal knife not unlike theCrystal Dart.[2]Though typically wielding equally massiveGolem's Halberd, some can be found carryingGolem Greatbowsthat they use with great precision.
Fire can be seen through the plates on their chests. Their hard, stone bodies are very resistant to physical damage, however they will topple if their ankles sustain enough damage, allowing for a critical attack on their chests.
Liurnia of the LakesCapital OutskirtsLeyndell, Royal CapitalLeyndell, Ashen CapitalMountaintops of the Giants
A golem carrying a massive halberd that it can use to tear the earth asunder and can eject streams of fire through their helmet. Be wary of the instance of this enemy on the cliffs just east of theMinor ErdtreeinGreyoll's Dragonbarrowthat wields a magically infused halberd, as it is extremely powerful and capable of using the halberd to summon three orbs that shoot a very destructive magical beam.
Surprising reach due to the length of their halberds, and they still have strong attacks to defend their weak ankles. When they are knocked down their chests are vulnerable for a critical hit but sometimes just continuing to hack away at the ankles may be more effective.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
A golem carrying a massive greatbow. It pulls back the hardy string with its immense strength to shoot great arrows infused with the storm.[3]Be wary of the Golems that guard the approach to theGreat Jarof Caelid, as their arrows unleash a magical explosion upon landing.
Almost defenceless at melee range since they can't point their bow further down at that point. The actual danger lies mostly in approaching them, after that the stomps should be of minimal difficulty.
A Golem found at the end ofHighroad Cave, having most likely fallen down from the bridge to theDivine Tower of Limgrave.
Damage types: mainlyStandarddamage, with somePiercedamage from its thrusts andFiredamage from its flame breaths.
It's immune to allStatus Effectsand has 40% negation to all non-Physicaldamage types except forMagic, where it has only 20% resistance. It is somewhat weak toStrikedamage, having 0% negation towards it, and a mild 10% negation against all other Physical damage types.
Since it starts out lying on the ground and will take a few seconds to get up once alerted, it's easy to get in some opening hits on its ankles. It has the range advantage and can hit most of the cave thanks to the length of its weapon.
The simplest strategy is to do the same as with a regular, non-boss halberd golem by sticking behind its ankles and backing away when its starts hitting the ground with the butt of its weapon or if it breaths fire.

name: Kindred of Rot | Elden Ring Wiki
Kindred of Rotis aField BossinElden Ring. These insect-like creatures wield a spear in their many arms and are found inSeethewater Cave. This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance inElden Ring.
Lesser Kindred of Rotis the normal enemy form of this boss. The spirit of a Kindred of Rot can be summoned for aid in battle usingKindred of Rot Ashes.
The end boss ofSeethewater Cave. [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
Buffed if any nearby character is poisoned, similar toKindred of Rot's Exultation
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Use theSwift Glintstone Shardspell to stagger them and stops them from using their thread attack
Keep your positioning to the side of them and focus on one at a time while rolling through any pest thread attacks. If you want a quick fight, use spirit summons to clear one while you clear the other. If you have a shield, you can guard counter them and it will stun them giving you more opportunities to deliver hits. Be patient and wait for an opening before coming down at them with by spamming your melee attacks, giving you an opportunity to interrupt their following attacks until they are cleared. Anticipate their next action and roll back if it follows through. Repeat the pattern of waiting for an opening until they are cleared.
Either Holy Damage or Faith Builds work when going against them. They tend to take long pauses before each action. Mages have the option to useSwift Glintstone Shard, which may interrupt their next action. If significant damage was taken, roll back and create a larger separation before healing. If this is difficult, and you are willing, use spirit summons to help you since there are two of them and may be hard to separate. Keeping your distance will give you more openings and will eventually lead to their defeat.

TheKindred of Rotorpestsareenemiesand optionalbossesinELDEN RING(2022).
Anthropomorphic, insectoid beings that emerged from theSwamp of Aeonia[1], they are forsaken servants and unwanted children of the newGoddess of Rot.[2][3]They are commonly found in places blighted byScarlet Rot, such asCaelidand theGrand Cloister.
Fully grown pests found in Rot-infested areas. They wield glaives made from hard, sharpened shell, and can fire web-like threads from a distance. If Scarlet Rot orPoisonis utilised near them, they receive a buff.
Fully-grown pests found in Rot-infested areas around theancient Rauh Ruinsand theChurch of the Bud. They are colored pink to signify they have been embraced byRomina, Saint of the Bud. They wield glaives made from hard, sharpened shell, and can firePest ThreadsandPest-Thread Spearsfrom a distance. If Scarlet Rot orPoisonis utilised near them, they receive a buff.

Misbegotten Warrioris an enemy inELDEN RING(2022). They are a variant of theMisbegottenenemies, appearing most often as bosses.
Hulking Misbegotten with long, red manes and serpentine tails. Misbegotten Warriors typically fight using large, iron greatswords. As with other Misbegotten, their appearance is seen as a punishment for making contact with the Primordial Crucible.[1]

name: Mad Pumpkin Head | Elden Ring Wiki
Mad Pumpkin Headis aField BossinElden Ring. These towering humanoids wield massive weapons and wear distinctive pumpkin-shaped helmets. These are optional bosses as players are not required to defeat them to advance inElden Ring.
Lesser Mad Pumpkin Headis the normal enemy form of this boss. Mad Pumpkin Heads can be summoned as spirits for aid in battle throughMad Pumpkin Head Ashes.
Though he has stifled his panic within the dark confines of his helmet, he rampages as if driven mad when agitated by bloodshed or the humming of insects. This mad soldier is all that is left of a broken gladiator.
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
While the flail variant's cant be parried, their punch attacks can be.
The head has extra armor, and attacks that hit it will do only 20% of base damage.
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Summon theLone Wolf Ashesto help stagger him, giving you an opening for free damage.
Attack from behind to avoid hitting his head.
After a sequence of slow but heavy attacks, he will slowly reposition himself before attacking again. This is your chance to punish him. When dodging his attacks, try to end up behind him so you can hit his unprotected back once he's finished.
Avoid shooting his head with spells or arrows. You can useSpirit Ashesto distract him so you can hit his back, or keep moving and rolling away to create enough distance to fire off spells or arrows.
UnderneathWaypoint Ruins. Head down a staircase in the center of the ruins, south of theGiant Miranda Sprout.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
This fight features two Mad Pumpkin Heads, one with a flail and the attacks described above, and one with a hammer and a different set of moves
Both Mad Pumpkin Heads must be defeated to win the fight
UnderneathCaelem Ruins. Head down a staircase in the southeast corner of the ruins, just north of a large bonfire.
Damage:Standard(Hammer),Standard,Strike(Flail)
If you put one Mad Pumpkin Head toSleepand wake it up without doing acritical hit, it will beat its chest three times before briefly turning against its ally.
UseSpirit Ashesto distract one Mad Pumpkin Head while you focus on the other.
Focus on the Mad Pumpkin Head wielding a hammer, since it has slower attacks. If they're both attacking you at once, make them chase you around the arena until one is blocking the other's way so you only have to worry about the one in front.
Mad Pumpkin Headis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
Gigantic humanoids with brawny physiques, known for their distinct oval helmets. They are former gladiators, broken and driven mad[1]. Their helmets are pitch black inside, intended to keep the warriors from panicking, and to alleviate feelings of pressure and claustrophobia.[2]
They typically wield hammers with crude, stone heads, or spikyChainlink Flails. Sometimes they can be seen carrying standards, which they will drive into the ground or throw at foes when initiating combat.
Their heads heavily reduce the damage of any attack that hits it.
