area: Limgrave
chapter: 1
name: Magma Wyrm | Elden Ring Wiki
Magma Wyrmis aField BossinElden Ring. Magma Wyrms were once human, but were transformed into lesser dragons for the sin ofDragon Communion. These are optional bosses as players are not required to defeat them to advance in Elden Ring.
See alsoMagma Wyrm MakarandGreat Wyrm Theodorix.
Those who have performed the Dragon Communion will find their humanity slowly slipping away. Once they fully succumb to their fate, they are left no more than wyrms that crawl the earth.
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
UseRedmane Knight Ogha Ashesfor his durability, fire resistance, and ranged attacks which can hit the Magma Wyrm's head for extra damage
If you don't have Ogha yet,Crystalian Ashes,Banished Knight Engvall Ashes, orBanished Knight Oleg Ashesare all effective for drawing (and surviving) aggresion
On the other hand,Ancestral Follower AshesandLatenna the Albinauricare useful for hitting its head for extra damage
Use theRock Slingspell to take advantage of its weakness to physical damage
UseFlamedrake Talismanto reduce fire damage
Heads I Win:Magma Wyrm takes more damage if you attack its head, so if you learn when it's vulnerable you can deal a lot of damage very quickly. Stay in front of it just far enough away to easily dodge its sword attacks but close enough to move in when it starts using Lava Belch. Avoid its sides if at all possible: it's hard to read its windups from there so its attacks can take you by surprise.
Tails You Lose:On the other hand, very few of its attacks can reliably or quickly hit directly behind it. If you focus on attacking its tail, you won't do as much damage but you won't have to work as hard to stay alive. If it starts to turn around, back up and move back in when you have a safe opportunity to run through its legs. Just be careful not to get boxed in by the lava it leaves lying on the ground.
Heads Up:Magic and ranged users have the advantage of being able to target its head at any time for extra damage. You can use quick-casting spells for added accuracy, or focus more on physical spells to take advantage of its relative lack of physical defense. Whatever you do, though, avoid fire damage because of its massive fire resistance.
Orbital Dynamics:Magma Wyrm doesn't rotate very quickly, so try to continue moving around it so it spends as much time as possible turning rather than attacking. This is particularly useful when you're using spirit summons: whenever it's focused on them, use that opportunity to stand on its opposite side to it has to rotate as much as possible once you draw its ire.
Magma Wyrms are individuals who have heavily partaken of Dragon Communion and degenerated into mere imiations of dragons.This is a recurring theme of Souls games, like in Dark Souls, there was a Dragon Cult built on worshipping and imitating the power of the Everlasting Dragons, and it is not too dissimilar here
Magma Wyrms have two additional sets of teeth that protrude from the roofs of their mouths, similar to the pterygoidal teeth of mosasaurs
The Magma Wyrms’ breath cannot knock players down.

Magma Wyrmis a reoccurringbossinELDEN RING(2022).
Magma Wyrms are quadrupedal draconic beings with torn, vestigial wings and broad heads. They were once human heroes who partook in Dragon Communion, for which they were cursed to crawl the earth[1]as flightless imitations of Dragons, losing their humanity in the process.[2]They wield greatswords that resemble the jawbones of dragons, and can spew magma from their mouths.
Only one non-boss Magma Wyrm can be encountered. It is found in the lower part ofVolcano Manor, accessible via an elevator near the Temple of Eiglay Site of Grace.

name: Onyx Lord | Elden Ring Wiki
Onyx Lordis aField BossinElden Ring.Onyx Lordsare a tall ancient race of humanoids with mastery over gravity magic that share a common background and appearance with theAlabaster Lords. This is an optional boss as players don't have to defeat it to advance inElden Ring.
Lesser Onyx Lordis the normalenemyform of this boss.
A race of ancients with skin of stone who were said to have risen to life when a meteor struck long ago. They were called lords in reverential fear of their destructive power.
Royal Grave Evergaol[More Info ↓] [Map Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance broken
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Fight him on the outer edges of the arena.
Take advantage of his Meteorite's long cast animation.
Onyx Lord only has a few moves in his repertoire and it is relatively easy to discern his patterns. Consider fighting him on the outer edges of the arena as the center has uneven terrain which can cause his meteorites to impact with the ground near you, dealing splash damage.
Onyx Lord has three main attack patterns: Meteorite, Slice and Dice, and Gravity Well. He will rarely diverge from these attacks. Meteorite has a very long animation and should be exploited. After he plunges his sword from the ground, you can try and get behind him for one or two hits. The meteors don't track very well at melee range and they are unlikely to hit you this way. His Gravity Orb attack comes out very quickly, has very good tracking and requires precise timing to dodge. His Slice and Dice move begins with a diagonal dash to his left as he slashes upwards followed by a large, sweeping slash in the opposite direction. Dodgingthroughthe first slash towards his right side should prevent the second slash from hitting you and will position you behind him for a quick counter.
Overall, his Meteorite and Slice and Dice moves are his most punishable for melee players.
Ranged players have the added advantage of being completely out of range of his sword plunge into Meteorite summon. Do note that he will sometimes charge towards you before he performs the plunge but the AoE is easy enough to avoid. The meteorites themselves have a slow travel speed and ranged/magic users should take this time to get a few hits in while they get ready to sidestep the projectiles. If you maintain your distance, the first slash of his Slice and Dice attack should land nowhere near you. However, this also makes you an easier target for the second slash. Try to dodge diagonally to the right after you see the first slash and then punish his recovery time accordingly.
The Onyx Lord in Royal Grave Evergaol was originally called "Alabaster Lord". The flavor text of Meteorite was also updated to reflect the change. The main difference between the two is their weaponry. Alabaster Lords wield greatswords, while Onyx Lords use curved greatswords.

Perfumer Tricia and Misbegotten Warrioris aField BossinElden Ring. Tricia is a spellcaster who prefers to remain at range and carries a shield, whileMisbegotten Warrioris an extremely agile creature wielding a greatsword. This is an optional bossfight, as players don't need to defeat them in order to advance inElden Ring.
Misbegotten Warriors also appears in theLeonine Misbegotten,Crucible Knight and Misbegotten Warrior, andMisbegotten Crusaderboss fights. Perfumer Tricia can be summoned for aid in battle by using thePerfumer Tricia Ashes.
See Perfumer Tricia and Misbegotten Warrior Lore
Tricia was once known as a healer who dedicated her efforts to treating Misbegotten, Omen, and all those seen as impure. When her efforts failed, she was their companion as they died, watching over them to ensure that they could pass peacefully, free of pain.
This fight features two enemies, both of whom must be defeated to win the fight

The Best Tips for Perfumer Tricia and Misbegotten Warrior:
Dodge or move to the side of the arena as soon as you enter the fog gate. The Misbegotten Warrior almost always lunges at the door when the fight begins. Wait until you are clear to use any summons if you are opting for that.
Use tanky Spirit Ashes or ones with good stagger such as theLone Wolf Ashesto distract the Misbegotten.
Get close to Tricia and pummel her with melee attacks to break her stance and get a critical attack in. Finish her off before your summons are killed.
This encounter has a steep difficulty due to the very aggressive, very powerful Misbegotten Warrior who will always close the distance. Tricia herself does not pose much of a threat as she will attempt to maintain distance and cast spells that hit in a wide arc from medium range. When the fight begins, summon your bestSpiritsin order to distract the Misbegotten and then immediately get up close to Tricia and pummel her with fast melee strikes. This will cause her to pull up her shield which does little to reduce damage from your constant barrage. It is also exceedingly easy to break her stance, setting her up for a highly damaging critical attack. Try to get rid of Tricia before your summons expire or get killed.
For the Misbegotten Warrior,do notattempt to create distance as the arena is relatively small and he has leaping attacks that travel a great distance. Whenever he swings horizontally, dodgethroughthe attack utilizing your roll's iframes instead of dodging backwards. Dodging backwards increases the time his sword's hitbox overlaps with your hitbox, causing a hit. This is especially important since he will likely have you with your back against the wall most of the time. Always try to get behind him and hit him once or twice. Do not get greedy. For his vertical slashes, always dodge sideways. In fact, the only time you should be dodging backwards is when he leaps to perform his slam attack, but even then, you should be moving diagonally.
Similarly to the Melee Strategy, do not attempt to create distance against the Misbegotten Warrior. Dodge through his attacks and use basic, quick-firing spells such asGlintstone Pebblewhen his back is turned. Consider using Melee-based Glintstone sorceries as well as these are typically cast much faster as a tradeoff for having little to no ranged capabilities. Just as with melee users, use a Spirit summon in the beginning and take Tricia out immediately to get her out of the way and then focus on the Misbegotten.

At ~50% health, does an AOE Scarlet Rot explosion. Run away and find a spot on the ground without a flame visual FX and stand still. If you attempt to keep running away, you may run into another scarlet rot explosion behind you.
Can be staggered, which is very effective as its head takes increased damage, and this makes it much more accessible while he is on the ground. Consider going for attacks directly on the head while it is stance broken, instead of a critical strike. Two main methods with melee are to constantly circle around its head when lowered or reach its tail and attack from there to avoid most of its directional attacks. Hug its back side since most attacks will come from the head. When it starts to pull back, be ready to dodge and dives or spontaneous movement dashes from the boss.Bloodhound's Stepcould be considered if available to dodge its quick attacks faster and to help with countering. Use a combination of waiting for its dive attacks, dodging through and repositioning around the beast to get as many hits in while out of its line of sight until HP is depleted. Keep an eye on yourScarlet Rot.
Can be burst down withMeteorite. As soon as you enter the fog door, target the boss and move right. It will try to attack. Immediately cast meteorite close to it and hold the button. It should stagger which allows you to drink a blue potion to replenish your FP. You might need enough FP for this to work. Another spell to consider isRock Sling, which deals great physical damage and can also stagger it.  If your FP is out and it doesn't stagger, you don't have enough Mind stat. Note: meteorite needs to be cast close to the target for it to hit. Though there is not a lot of free space in the arena where this boss is found so creating distance for longer ranged attacks will be a challenge. To aid with this, it is recommended to useSpirit Ashesduring this encounter. Continue your attacks in between the windows of this boss's attack until it is defeated.

To open this door, move past the spirits fighting one another and head up the second flight of stairs on the north, jog east, and then head north again through the tunnel past the room with two spirits. Turn east at the corner, run through the next room, then turn south at the next corner. In this room, you'll see a knight sitting at the other end, but instead of running up to it, jump through the window to the west onto a ledge below. Head up the stairs, then jump through another window to the west which opens onto the platform with the lever.

Royal Revenantis an enemy inELDEN RING(2022).
Pale, gaunt creatures resembling corpses with many limbs. They emerge from pools of shallow water, and attack with unnatural speed and the ability to inflictPoison.
They take damage from and are stunned by healing incantations such asHeal,Great Heal,Lord's HealandErdtree Heal, losing half their health if hit. They also take damage from healing over time incantations, such asBlessing's BoonandBlessing of the Erdtree, losing 90% of their health over 30 seconds if affected by such as spell.
They are often accompanied byRevenant Followers.
A Royal Revenant encountered in the hidden cellar of Kingsrealm Ruins in north-westernLiurnia of the Lakes. It guards a chest containing theFrozen Needle.
Encountered in a very small room and without having to go through their signature lengthy spawning animation, this Revenant will turn aggressive quickly.
If it leaps towards roll forwards to the left of it and get in a hit before backing away, being ready to roll. Should it start to use more short-ranged melee slams, back away to provoke more leaps. Sometimes it will start to chain these slams into one long combo, either try to keep as far away as possible from this or get behind it if already close.
Occasionally it will start to emit a green color around its head which signifies that it's about to spit out a thin cone ofPoisonsludge. Potentially dangerous if caught in the middle of an action such as drinking aFlask of Crimson Tearsbut otherwise easily rolled or jumped away from.
Sometimes it will slip through a portal underground to appear behind its target and spit poison before starting its attack routine again.
One easy way to kill it is to find an opening to cast a cheap healing spell such asHealand then cast it again immediately while it's stunned. Any class can do this as even aPrisonerhas enoughFaithwith aCommoner's Garb/Commoner's Simple GarbandTwo Fingers Heirloom.

name: Stonedigger Troll | Elden Ring Wiki
Stonedigger Trollis aBossinElden Ring. ThisElden Ring Stonedigger Troll Guidefeatures boss locations, tips, strategies and videos on how to defeat Stonedigger Trolls easily, as well as boss stats and lore for the Stonedigger Trolls.
Trolls are tall humanoid creatures with a distinctive hole in their chests. They are descendants of the Giants, who were mortal enemies of the Erdtree, yet in the War against the Giants, they fought for the Golden Order against their brethren. Some trolls are also loyal to the Carian royal family - these Troll knights can be found carrying theTroll Knight's Sword. The stone hammer that the Stonedigger Trolls carry were ceremonial relics used in smithing, an act that was once seen as divine.
This is an optional boss, as players don't need to defeat it in order to advance. These towering creatures may have a tough exterior, but they can be easily toppled; beware of their high level ofHardness, but overcome it and they are easily staggered.Sleepis also effective for this fight due to the Troll's low resistance to the status effect. They drop theRoar MedallionandGreat Clubwhen defeated.
Bosses are unique and challengingEnemiesthat can be encountered all over the Lands Between. Great Enemy bosses can drop uniqueSpirit Ashes,Weapons,Spells, and other variousItems.
Trollscan be found as a regular enemy in the Lands Between.
Trolls are descended from the giants, and their hammers were supposedly once used as ceremonial smithing tools. In the distant past, smithing was considered divine.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
Use theKaiden Sellsword Ashesfor an easier fight orSpirit Jellyfish Ashesas a distraction.
The Troll is extremely weak toSleep. A singleSleep Potwill put it to sleep no matter how low your Arcane or how many times it's already slept.
The Troll has highHardness, so most one-handed melee attacks will rebound off it preventing you from landing chain attacks. You can prevent this by two-handing your weapon or using a weapon with higher Hardness. Also, beware of its large area-of-effect attacks and give yourself plenty of time to move out of the way or roll through them. Otherwise, the safest place to be is near his feet, and ideally behind him as well. You can still get hit by his Stomp, but follow-up moves will mostly miss you.
Stance Breaking:Since the troll has very lowStance, it doesn't take many fully-charged heavy attacks or jump attacks to get it to collapse onto the floor. Land acritical hitif you want, or just land more blows until it gets back up.
The Troll is slow but hits with large area-of-affect attacks, so make sure you aren't caught in them. It's best to use a shield in one hand and your staff or seal in the other, in case you need to guard in an emergency. Bait his attacks, then roll away to create separation before casting.
The Stonedigger Trolls wield theTroll's Hammer, a ceremonial smithing tool, suggesting that they used to be blacksmiths. In the distant past, smithing was considered divine. The hammer is also used byWar Counselor Iji, a Troll blacksmith who used to serve the Carian royals.

Trolls are descendants of the Giants[1], who betrayed their ancestors during the war against the Giants[2]and fought on behalf of theErdtree.[3]They can be found throughout theLands Between, often fighting on behalf of various armies and factions. They have broad torsos, with cavities in their chests exposing growths akin to roots or branches, which conceal stone stabs that were seemingly embedded into them. Sometimes, stakes are lodged into these cavities, allowing the trolls to drag carriages along behind them.

The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
UseOrder HealingandLaw of Regressionfor curing
BringPrince of Death's PustuleorPrince of Death's CystTalismans
BringImmunizing Cured Meatconsumable forDeath Blightmitigation
BringRejuvenating Bolusesused solely to Alleviate death blight buildup
As a melee user you are susceptible to whenever it performs its mid rangedDeath Blightattacks so you will have to be extra vigilant. When anticipating its spewing and cloud release. Try to have larger trees to your side to have something to duck behind. To quickly deplete its health as a melee user, as much as possible you can hug this creatures feat, but circle behind so it cant grab you and deal your series of attacks on its legs from behind. This creature has one of the more slower moving actions but its attacks deal great effects so be careful when running in. Run in between attacks and keep to its legs from behind so you are out of range to be affected by melee attacks as well. Keep focusing on hitting its legs until it is defeated. Bring extra talismans that can mitigate death blight for more aid andRejuvenating Bolusesto decrease buildup.
Keeping at long range against this boss may invite it to also counter with its main long rangedDeath Blightattack. Getting hit by this puke attack causes serious damage and serious Death Blight buildup. Since it is encountered in the open world, use large trees to your advantage to avoid its effects. At mid range, you can also still be affected by the cloud AoE it releases. This moves relatively slowly so back away as this approaches. At this range the wormface may also attempt to run at you. It isn't a very quick dash however it closes the distance very quickly and then will usually follow up with an attempt to grab. From here, circle away from its grasps, if you would like at this point, temporarily switch to melee to get some hits on its legs. Since it doesn't have the fastest actions, with ranged combat wait for its attacks to and and deal an attack of your own in between each completed action until its HP has depleted. UseOrder HealingandLaw of Regressionfor curing if available.
The file names for the Wormfaces are Deracine_Male for the small ones, and Deracine_Female for the large ones.Deracine could come from a French word for uprooting trees, or it could mean “displaced.”
Just northwest of theMinor Erdtree (Altus Plateau). From theBower of BountySite of Grace, head east along the path, then turn north towards the Minor Erdtree. Once you reach the tree, circle clockwise around it until you reach the Wormface. [Map Link]

The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
This enemy does not have a boss bar, but it will not respawn when killed
Disguised as aBurning Putrid Corpsestanding by a bonfire just east of theRoad of IniquitySite of Grace. Once you kill the Putrid Corpse, it'll transform into the Wormface. [Map Link]
Towering, emaciated creatures with worm-like tentacles protruding from their faces. They regularly cough up clouds ofDeath Blightwhich cover a large area around them. The majority of them reside in the woodlands of theAltus Plateau, however there are also several of them residing inCrumbling Farum Azula.
The smaller variety of Wormface, typically seen carrying ornate, wooden batons which they use in combat. Some wear faded yellow cloaks.
Much larger Wormfaces. They do not wield weapons, instead using headbutts, grabs, and Death Blight in combat.
One can be found on Mt. Gelmir, near the Road of Iniquity Site of Grace. Initially it appears to be aBurning Putrid Corpse, but if it is killed or blows itself up, it will transform into a Giant Wormface. It drops aLarval Tearupon defeat.

Count Ymir, Mother of Fingersis aBossinElden Ring. Count Ymir, Mother of Fingers is the High Priest who has taken power fromMetyr, Mother of Fingers, and is found in theCathedral of Manus Metyr. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance in Elden Ring.
To defeat this boss, you must first defeat an invasion fromSwordhand of Night Jolan, then defeat Ymir himself
This is a Tarnished boss: its stats and attacks work like a player character with equipped items
Closest Site of Grace:Cathedral of Manus Meyr
Count Ymir, Mother of Fingers can be found in the Cathedral of Manus Metyr once you've defeatedMetyr, Mother of Fingers. Interact with the throne, and the boss fight will begin. [Map Link]
Armor:High Priest Hat,High Priest Robe,High Priest Gloves,High Priest Undergarments
Drops210,000,Ymir's Bell Bearing,Maternal Staff,High Priest Set
Thedefensenumbers are compared to the incoming attack power to determine how much to scale down the damage. The higher the ratio, the more damage comes through.
Thenegationnumbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through a nd 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
Weapons:Sword of Night(right),Shield of Night(left)

The Best Tips for Count Ymir, Mother of Fingers:
Use spells that do Lightning damage, such asLightning Spear
Equip fast-hitting weapon types, such asHand-to-Hand ArtsandFists
Use weapons or spells that dealFire Damageto quickly deal with the summonedFingercreepers.
Count Ymir, Mother of Fingerscan be encountered in theCathedral of Manus Metyr. After defeatingMetyr, Mother of Fingers, return to the Cathedral of Manus Metyr and interact with the throne again. Jolán will first invade, then Count Ymir will appear after she is defeated. This boss dealsMagic Damageand can summons allies.
The stars are dark tonight. But rest assured, this is no ill omen. On the contrary. I believe that this portends a magnificent starry cascade.
Count Ymir, High Priest, later known asYmir, Mother of Fingers, is acharacterinShadow of the Erdtree.
Ymir is a glintstone sorcerer[1]who resides in theCathedral of Manus Metyr. Ymir once instructedRellana, a princess of theCarian Royal Family, however he abandoned his alliegence to the moon, believing it to be merely the closest of the celestial bodies.[2]He is served byJolán, Swordhand of Night, who is fiercely loyal to her count.[3]
Ymir possesses insight into the nature of the world, claiming that we are children of theGreater Will, born as stardust from a rapture far across the skies.[4]He believes thatQueen Marika, theTwo Fingers, and theirmotherhave been defective from the start.[5]Ymir himself aspires to become a mother of fingers.[6]When theTarnishedmeets Ymir, he gives them ahollowed-out stone necklaceand tasks them with sounding the bells at the Finger Ruins ofRhiaandDheo. After the bells have been rung, Ymir sends them to theFinger Ruins of Miyr, located below the cathedral, to sound the final bell. Doing so transports them to another place, where they encounter and defeatMetyr, Mother of Fingers. Following this, Ymir succeeds in becoming a mother of Fingers himself and attacks the Tarnished, only to be defeated.
Count Ymir's questline is tied to that ofJolán, Swordhand of Night. Proceeding with certain quest stages may lock you out of any rewards.
At the end of his questline, Ymir can be fought. He will use spells from theFinger-Weaversand spawn 3Fingercreepersfrom time to time.

name: Demi-Human Swordmaster Onze | Elden Ring Wiki
Demi-Human Swordmaster Onzeis aGreat Enemy BossinElden Ring. Onze is a demi-human that, despite his appearance, skillfully wields a magic katana and is found at the bottom of theBelurat Gaol. This is an optional boss as players don't need to defeat it to advance inShadow of the Erdtree.
Demi-Human Swordmaster Onze can be found at the bottom of theBelurat Gaol. Players will find the entrance to this area by going to the lake east of theBelurat Tower Settlement. Players will see cages and traps along the way that will lead to a small entrance to the location. To reach the boss location, look for the section where you see crock pots suspended in the air with chains. Jump down these platforms and navigate the area until you see the yellow mist door on the south side. See theDemi-Human Swordmaster Onzeon the [Elden Ring Shadow of the Erdtree Map] [Video Link]
Is vulnerable to acritical hitafter beingstance brokenor parried
The negation numbers are the % of your damage that gets blocked. For example, if a negation is 60, 40% of that damage by that type will go through and 60% will be negated. Bigger number = less damage. A negation of 100 means no damage goes through, and a negation of -100 mean the enemy takes 2x damage from that source. 0 means damage goes pretty much as is.
The resistance numbers are the buildup amount to trigger it. For example, if a resistance is 100 you must deal 100 points of the given buildup to trigger it. Note that these go down over time, and increase each time the effect procs. The values after the "/"s indicate the increased resistances after each successive proc.
The Best Tips for Demi-Human Swordmaster Onze:
Summons:Black Knife Tiche,Mimic Tear,Greatshield Soldier Ashes
The boss is a small creature that can move nimbly. They can outmaneuver you in combat and sneak up behind you with their fast movement. This boss, however, can be staggered and their poise can be broken by repeatedly hitting them. You can also summon Spirit Ashes likeBlack Knife Tiche. Their attacks will apply stagger and their quick movement will allow them to keep up with the boss fight. Alternatively, you can also summonGreatshield Soldier Ashesto force the boss into a corner, or you can opt for aGreatshieldto absorb attacks from this boss.
While fighting this boss, make sure to keep your target locked on them so they don't sneak up on you. This also lets you be on guard for any of their attacks. Despite their quick movement, their slashes are comparatively slow because of the wind-up. He holds up his weapon for a few frames before launching the attack and lets you predict their next move. You can alternate going offense and defense by holding up your shield when he's attacking, and then attacking him when he pulls back. This should give you a few frames to attack him while he's not jumping around. This boss can easily be staggered with light and heavy attacks.
The boss will begin the fight with a move calledMagic Slash. He will teleport midair in front of the player and will slash downward to bring forth magical damage in a small area. You can dodge this attack by rolling backward, or to your right. We recommend the latter to close the gap and land a free heavy attack. There's a short pause after the move that lets you hit him freely and you can cut off the rest of his attack pattern.
Another move that is worth mentioning is theOrb Cuts. He usually does this when you attempt an attack while he's guarding, and you will see him raise his sword above his head and stabs forward to create an orb around him. This generates an energy that cuts anything within the area. Similar to theWaterfowl Dancebut, the boss will stay only in one place. This means that you can dodge this attack by rolling backward.
He has about 3 Magic attacks aside from hisStandard Sword attacks. The magic ones are deadlier than his attacks, make sure to keep an eye on his sword if it's glowing blue, or white. When you get the chance, attempt to strike him from behind repeatedly to break his poise. With the help of any spirit summons, this fight shouldn't take long.
Use spirit summons like Tiche who can keep up with Onze’s speed as he will dart around the space for the duration of the battle. While Tiche is engaged, use quick spells like Glintstone pebble. If Onze is focused on you, be patient and dodge until your spirit summons can take aggro again. He will raise his blade or jump into the air to indicate an attack is coming which makes dodging a simple task.Onze is most vulnerable from behind and will take more damage from the back. With a spirit summons, this battle should be fairly simple.
Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.Use to summon the spirit of Yosh, the demi-human swordsman.
Onze, a master swordsman who devoted himself to the Star-Lined Sword, realized that only ruin awaited at the end of the procession of stars, and imprisoned himself in order to forestall it.
However, Yosh, an apprentice who absorbed his technique, stubbornly refused to heed his master's words, and spent his entire life at his side, in defiance of his self-imposed seclusion.
Sword encrusted with a line of stars fashioned from small pieces of crude glintstone. Weapon of the demi-human swordsmen.
When bestowed with this weapon by their queen, the swordsmen swear to find the truth that lies at the end of the procession of stars.
Glintstone staff styled as a scepter. A gift once given to the demi-humans to foster peace, it can be wielded even by those of low intelligence.
Demi-Human Swordmaster Onzeis an optionalbossinShadow of the Erdtree. He is encountered at theBelurat Gaol.
In a bygone era, whenbeastswere granted intelligence,[1][2]thedemi-humanswordsmenwere bequeathedStar-Lined Swordsby theirqueens.[3]Their royal blades were encrusted with shards of crude glintstone, symbolizing theprocession of the stars.[4]Each swordsman swore an oath to unveil the secret that awaited at the end of the line of stars.
Onze was a master swordsman who devoted himself to theStar-Lined Sword.[5]When Onze realized that only ruin awaited at the end, he imprisoned himself in order to forestall it.[5]His devoted apprentice,Yosh, defied him and spent the remainder of his days in hermitage by his side.[6]
Onze is an elderly demi-human swordsmen, small in stature with mottled, pale skin. He wears a filthy loincloth and a tattered cape clasped with rope. He has five fingers. His milky eyes are fully clouded over and thin wisps of white hair hang from his scalp and chin. Despite his withered appearance, he is nimble and deadly with his magical sword.

area: Limgrave

name: Tree Sentinel
Tree Sentinelis a reoccurring boss inELDEN RING(2022).
An order of knights, dedicated to the protection of theErdtree.[1]They are considered to be the living rampart of the Erdtree, and served as inspiration for Leyndell's knights.[2]
After the Ancient Dragon Gransax attacked Leyndell, some of the Tree Sentinels began to emulate the Ancient Dragons in order to better protect the Erdtree[3], wielding weapons[4]and shields[5]whittled from the claws of dragons and imbued with their lightning. These knights are referred to asDraconic Tree Sentinels.
A Tree Sentinel who wields a halberd and a greatshield. The shield allows the Tree Sentinel to dispel sorceries and counter with a golden beam that deals holy damage.
Can include a separate table for a specific instance of this variant's moveset.
A Tree Sentinel that wields a halberd and a torch, the latter dealing fire damage when used to attack.
A duo of Tree Sentinels found in theHinterlandsofScaduview, guarding the path to theMinor Erdtreeincantation.
The shield-wielder starts out on to the left, on the path to riding across the nearby bridge, while the torch-wielder is riding down the path fromShaman Village. This means they are quite easy to fight separately.
